Norway Occupies Greenland Island

Danish Government Considers it a Violation of Agreements

National News Agency, Oslo, 12th - Despite the dispute between Norway and Denmark over southeastern Greenland being subject to adjudication by the International Court of Justice in The Hague, the Norwegian government has now implemented an occupation because Denmark is sending a large team of scientists to survey and map the disputed area. According to the Norwegian government's subsequent explanation, the Danish survey team sent to eastern Greenland this year was given police powers. Furthermore, in recent years, Denmark has attempted to prevent whaling ships from landing in Greenland. Another report claims that the Norwegian government took this action because Denmark sent a police force to occupy southeastern Greenland. The area that the Norwegian government has decided to occupy is between 60 degrees 30 minutes and 63 degrees 40 minutes north latitude. Last year, a Norwegian expedition surveyed the area and mapped part of it.

National News Agency, Copenhagen, 13th - The Danish government and people are extremely concerned upon hearing the news of Norway's occupation of parts of Greenland. Prime Minister Stauning declared that the government considers Norway's actions not only as an infringement of Danish rights as in similar actions last year, but also a violation of the 1924 agreement and an infringement on Danish territory, as the area is part of Finland's colony in Greenland. He added that the matter will be handled through foreign affairs to be rectified through proper diplomatic channels.

Spain

Latest Warship Runs Aground and Sinks

National News Agency, Madrid, 12th - The Spanish warship 'Blas de Lezo' ran aground near Cape Finisterre today and sank immediately. Fortunately, there was no loss of life. The ship was built in 1923 and was the newest and fastest ship in the Spanish navy.

Large Anthracite Coal Mine Discovered in Italy

Sufficient for 150 Years of Use

National News Agency, Rome, 12th - It is reported that a large anthracite coal mine has been discovered in the Vasio Valley at the foot of the Alps in northern Italy. Experts estimate that the coal reserves total 100 million tons, which is sufficient to meet Italy's needs for a long time. Italy's coal production is limited, only one million tons per year. This new mine can support Italy for at least 150 years.

Special Tax Levied on Irish Goods Imported into Britain

To Be Implemented Starting Today

Irish Government Plans Retaliation

Reuters, London, 12th - The Special Tax on Free State Goods Act will now be implemented, allowing the British government to recover the £3 million per year owed by the Free State in land annuities. The Treasury Department issued an order tonight stating that, starting July 14th, the following goods imported into Britain from the Free State will be subject to a 20% ad valorem tax: livestock, butter, eggs, beef, pork, poultry, game, and various meats.

Reuters, Dublin, 13th - All of Ireland was astonished to hear that the British government had decided to impose a special tax on Irish imports, as the initial understanding was that this would not happen before the arbitration issue was resolved. It is feared that arbitration may be difficult to achieve. Free State cabinet members held a secret meeting last night, where there was talk of imposing retaliatory tariffs. Former Free State President Cosgrave told a Reuters reporter today that the poor farmers would rely on divine help. A Free State MP claimed today that if someone had 3,000 head of cattle for export, they would lose £12,000 in British gold under the new tax regulations.

Belgian Strike Wave Difficult to Resolve

Workers Put Forward Three Demands

Reuters, Brussels, 12th - A general strike has broken out in the Liège region due to a labor dispute in the coal industry. Police are making every effort to maintain order, and there has been no unrest so far. Disputes have also occurred in the Charleroi area, with approximately 2,000 people arrested. Other areas are peaceful, but a resolution to the strike seems unlikely at present.

National News Agency, Brussels, 12th - The General Committee of the Belgian Socialist Party and the Executive Committee of the National Trade Union, unexpectedly vetoed a motion to declare a general strike, instructing workers in areas not affected by the labor unrest to continue working as before. However, they expressed full support for all the demands made by the striking workers, requesting the Belgian government to comply. The main points raised by the workers are: (1) Abandon the proposal to increase wheat prices, (2) Immediately stop wage cuts, (3) Ensure that those who wish to work have the opportunity to do so.

Shoe King

Died After Not Entering Sleeping Cabin

Known as the "Ford" of Europe During His Lifetime

National News Agency, Prague, 12th - Regarding the circumstances of the death of Czech millionaire shoe king Bata, we have now received a detailed telegram stating that before Bata's private plane took off, the pilot refused to depart due to the heavy fog. However, Bata insisted on going, so the pilot took off and ascended. After ascending into the sky, they saw that the surroundings were filled with fog and there was no way to proceed. Therefore, they descended, but during the descent, they touched the wires of a high-voltage power line, causing the accident. Bata's plane had a sleeping cabin, but after boarding the plane, Bata lost his usual behavior and did not enter the sleeping cabin, but sat with the pilot. Otherwise, Bata would not have died, as Bata's sleeping cabin was completely undamaged.

Havas, Czech Capital, 12th - Bata was highly respected by people here during his lifetime. Upon hearing of his death, people near and far mourned him. Bata was the son of a Moravian shoemaker. He inherited his father's trade and, relying on his efforts, was able to expand his father's business. In 1930, he managed 32 shoe factories and employed 16,000 workers, so he was sometimes referred to as the "Ford" of Europe.

Important News

Northeastern Traitors

Eagerly Seeking to Expand Military Strength

Recruiting New Soldiers from Villages

Purchasing Guns from Civilians

Japanese Forcibly Implementing Education Plans

Yu Zhishan's Troops Serving as Accomplices

North China Correspondence: A person from the Northeast discussed the recent situation in the Northeast as follows: (1) Northeastern rebels, such as Zhang Haipeng's troops, have recently been actively recruiting new soldiers from villages. However, apart from a few unemployed vagrants who have responded to the call, the rest of the villagers are unwilling to join. The rebels are also carrying a large number of propaganda materials to promote among the villagers, spreading fallacies such as, [At the beginning of the establishment of Manchuria, the national defense is not yet consolidated. We hope that patriotic people will quickly enlist to protect the national defense.] (2) The Japanese have recently been actively investigating the number of households and fixed assets in each village, and plan to purchase all civilian guns in order to form a military. This order to collect guns was issued to the village chiefs of each village a few days ago, setting a deadline for payment: 30 yuan for large guns and 40 yuan for small guns. They are also instructing each village to build walls and repair fences in order to defend against bandits. (3) The Japanese army is extremely tyrannical in each village. If farmers slightly violate their established rules, they will be shot. Recently, when trains on the Datong Road arrive at Badaohao, the Japanese army swarms up and searches passengers extensively, taking the opportunity to steal passengers' belongings. The Japanese soldiers stationed in Xinlitun are demolishing all the houses near them because the weather is getting hotter, in order to allow air to circulate. (4) The Japanese supervisors of the Puppet Education Department have recently been frequently convening meetings of the principals and teachers of various schools, forcibly ordering them to implement the Japanese education plan, and ordering students of various schools to organize youth league groups affiliated to the Concordia Association (the Concordia Association is a group of Japanese invaders in the Northeast). All the work of the group is under the control of the Concordia Association. Its purpose is to promote the recognition of the puppet Manchuria and often sends people to give lectures in various counties and villages to deceive the people. (5) The Shenyang Japanese Gendarmerie recently summoned Wei, the head of the Puppet Education Department, accusing him of not working hard to build Japanese language schools, and ordered him to establish Japanese language schools in all counties in the shortest possible time in accordance with the order. (6) Yu Zhishan's rebellious troops recently occupied civilian farmland outside the West Gate of Beishancheng Town to build an airfield, with an area of more than 1,000 mu. The Japanese Kwantung Leased Territory requested 20 aircraft to be allocated to them, and they fly to various places every day to scout out the activities of the National Salvation Army. On the 4th of this month, more than 2,000 troops of the brigade, along with 300 Japanese artillery soldiers and six Japanese aircraft, advanced towards Chaoyang Town and engaged in a fierce battle with the 2,000 troops of the National Salvation Army led by Li Qiankun in the area. The Japanese aircraft dropped incendiary bombs, and the entire town was engulfed in flames, destroying countless houses. In order to preserve their strength, the National Salvation Army completely withdrew to nearby areas to wait for an opportunity to counterattack.

Another report: A person from Qingyuan said that Guan Xiangyang's National Salvation Army, with more than 10,000 soldiers, and Li Jingyang, the commander-in-chief of the White Flag Society, led more than 1,000 members of the White Flag Society and clashed with more than 2,000 of Yu Zhishan's troops led by Sun, the puppet chief of staff, in Nanshancheng Town on the 6th of this month. After a day of fierce fighting, Yu's troops were unable to withstand the attack and retreated into the city. The National Salvation Army attacked from all sides and heavily besieged the city. Yu Zhishan is currently in Beishancheng Town. Because the National Salvation Army is powerful, he sent an urgent telegram to the Japanese Kwantung Leased Territory. On the 7th, the Japanese sent five aircraft to assist, flying to various places from 8 a.m. to 6 p.m. every day to scout and bomb. However, the National Salvation Army is determined to fight and relies on strategic locations to fight without retreating. As of the 8th, Yu's troops in Nanshancheng Town had not yet escaped danger. (10th)

Korean Patriotic Corps

Plotting to Bomb Important Japanese Figures

Still Dispatched by Kim Koo

Targeting Honjo et al.

Four People, Including Liu and Cui, Arrested

Bombs Also Shaped Like Water Bottles

Seoul Correspondence: According to the Kyung Sung Nippo newspaper of the 3rd of this month, Korean Patriotic Corps members Liu Sang-geun, Choi Heung-shik, Lee Seong-won, and Lee Seong-bal planned to assassinate Kantogun Commander Honjo Shigeru and South Manchurian Railway President and newly appointed Foreign Minister Uchida Kosai when the League of Nations Investigative Delegation arrived at Dalian Station from Shenyang and Japanese military and government officials personally greeted them. The local police station discovered the plan and arrested Liu and the other four, but kept it secret. It was not until the beginning of this month that the newspapers were allowed to report it. Here is a translation of the general outline:

Since the Manchurian Incident occurred and Japan implemented its invasion of the three northeastern provinces of China, the Korean Independence Party believed that the spark for the Second World War had been ignited and was actively planning a restoration movement on a large scale with careful planning. The Korean Patriotic Corps, led by Kim Koo, was solely responsible for assassination. Before the outbreak of the Shanghai War, the organization had already dispatched violent elements to various places one after another, seeking opportunities to act. The Japanese authorities learned of this information early on, so they secretly deployed security lines in various places in Japan and Korea. The corps disregarded the sacrifices and on January 8th of this year, member Lee Bong-chang threw a bomb at the Japanese Emperor in Tokyo. On April 29th, they sent Yoon Bong-gil to throw special bombs at military and government officials at the Shanghai Japanese celebration of Tencho-setsu at Hongkou Park, and all eight people, including Shirakawa and Shigemitsu, were not spared. Afterwards, military police in various parts of Japan increased their vigilance, almost to the point of sleeplessness and sleeplessness, and they suspected that the corps was roaring, and even the movement of grass and trees was regarded as the corps' activities, making it impossible to defend against. On April 29th, the Dalian Post Office discovered a Korean throwing a letter with a Chinese-style secret telegram number. It was immediately sent to the police station in the port for inspection. It was only then that it was learned that there were several assassins lurking in the port, preparing to take action. Therefore, the entire city was searched. At dawn on May 24th, Choi Heung-shik was arrested at the home of Kim Jeong-soon, a Korean fisherman at No. 5, Beitashan Tong, in the Korean Fishermen's Association. The next day, Liu Sang-geun, Lee Won-seong, and Lee Won-bal were arrested one after another. After severe torture, the truth became clear. It is said that the four were all Koreans and were ordered by Kim Koo, the leader of the Patriot Corps. Choi Heung-shik (22 years old) was quick-witted and good at planning, and was solely responsible for investigating the security situation in Lushun and Dalian. On April 1st, he sneaked into Dalian by sea and hid in the home of Kim Jeong-soon in the Korean dormitory of the South Manchurian Railway, Kodama Ryo. During this period, he secretly went to Fengtian, Changchun, and Harbin to find opportunities. Liu Sang-geun (age 𠃒)

Assassination mission. On May 4th, he came to Dalian from a certain place and hid in the bedroom of a Korean employee of the South Manchurian Railway in the Kodama Ryo dormitory in Koyamacho. Lee Yong-bal, the eldest son of a 72-year-old man, Lee Seong-won and Seong-bal, were responsible for transporting weapons. Bombs and pistols were transported from a certain place by boat to Yingkou and then transferred to Dalian and delivered to Liu Sang-geun for storage. Liu received the weapons and hid them in his own suitcase. The four secretly communicated and made arrangements. They learned that the League of Nations Investigative Delegation would arrive at Dalian Station at 7:40 p.m. on May 26th. Honjo Shigeru and Uchida Kosai, who came here in advance to wait, would personally greet them at the time. They attempted to take the opportunity to bomb and annihilate the two in one fell swoop. If the opportunity was missed, they would change the date to 3:30 a.m. on the 30th when the investigation delegation left Dalian. After the purpose was achieved, they would commit suicide with the prepared pistols and would never allow the Japanese to capture them. After Liu Sang-geun was arrested, his attitude was calm. Choi Heung-shik said that he did not care about the failure this time, because his comrades were spread all over the place, dedicated to killing the Japanese giants who had ambitions. They would continue to advance and never stop the implementation of this plan. According to the confession, their purpose this time was to give a severe punishment to those who destroyed the peace of the East in front of the eyes of the investigation delegation and to make the international community understand that the Korean people's resistance to the strong Japanese was on the same front as China, and not like the Japanese unilateral deceptive propaganda, blindly obscuring the world's vision. It is said that the bomb copied by the police station is of the same type as the bomb used by Bai Chuan et al. in Hongkou Park. It is a large military water bottle weighing 130 taels containing strong explosives and thin white iron, wrapped in a 3-fen thick steel skin, lined with yellow flannel, and tied with a long belt. When throwing it, remove the small cap and pull out the tip. This tip can generate friction and ignite naturally. Moreover, because the water bottle-shaped bomb is tied with a long belt, it can use centrifugal force to adjust the distance according to the distance of the purpose, which is extremely accurate. (China United Press)

Ministry of Navy

Requests Investigation of Gao You-tang

Claims Gao Damaged Military Reputation and Violated Regulations

Supervisory Committee Member Gao You-tang recently made remarks to news reporters in Jinan, which involved the navy. The Ministry of Navy now believes that Gao has violated the provisions of Article 10 of the Impeachment Law, intentionally damaging the military's reputation, confusing the regulations of the council, and violating regulations. It has submitted a document to the government yesterday requesting an investigation. The full text is as follows:

[Submitting a request for the investigation of Supervisory Yuan member Gao You-tang, who has damaged the military's reputation, shaken the people's hearts, confused the council's regulations, and violated regulations. I respectfully request your approval. I have read in the Shanghai Shen Bao on the 9th of this month that Supervisory Yuan member Gao You-tang made remarks in Jinan. One of them stated that the impeachment case against the Ministry of Navy will also be submitted to the Central Government. Because of the Shanghai War, the 19th Route Army advanced bravely, while the navy stood by idly and signed a treaty with Japanese Admiral Shiiozawa,

Page 10

Agreeing that shells would not land on naval ships and that no shots would be fired. The 19th Route Army asked to borrow anti-aircraft guns but was refused, and even a single iron plate was not lent. It is too unbearable. The corruption on weekdays is unspeakable. The Marine Corps is not on the ships but is planting opium in Fujian, relying on its power to oppress the people. Director Yu often said, why bother to use the blood, sweat, and money of the people of the country to maintain the rice bowls of the people of Fujian? Because the current navy has become the world of the hereditary Fujian people. We advocate that the navy be completely abolished and that the ships be sold to merchants as merchant ships, because the navy's annual fee is more than one million, which is equivalent to having no navy. Why not free up this amount and add the proceeds from the sale of the ships to purchase 200 submarines? It should be known that the Chinese navy does not hope to attack people, but it is much better to defend the sea with 200 small boats than with useless warships. In addition, the Capital New Kyoto Daily also published the member's remarks, stating that the impeachment case against Navy Minister Chen Shaokuan was again being considered. The navy's monthly expenses require one million yuan, which is not insignificant. However, it cannot defend the country and resist foreign aggression, and coastal merchant ships are often robbed. The navy has not heard of any plans to suppress them, which is extremely shameful. The Marine Corps is forcibly planting chestnuts in Fujian, sucking the marrow of the people. What is the use of such troops? Therefore, it is suggested that the Central Government abolish the navy and use this huge sum of one million yuan per month to purchase 200 submarines. After all, it is better to use submarines to maintain the coastal defense than to be unable to fight and resist the enemy. I have investigated that Gao You-tang's impeachment of the navy has been reported in the newspapers more than once. The Ministry did not want to engage in meaningless debate and tolerated it again and again. However, the member has become more and more arrogant, even making speeches everywhere slandering the central government agencies to show off his ability to impeach and serve as a source of conversation. The remarks he made were all deliberately provocative and insulting to the government. Now, I will correct the slanderous remarks about the navy: One, the navy stood by idly during the Shanghai War, and anti-aircraft guns and steel plates were not lent. Since China and Japan have not formally declared war, how dare the navy act without government orders? As for the navy's purchase of military equipment and ammunition, reports have been filed. Whether there are anti-aircraft guns and steel plates that can be allocated and borrowed is already under the government's assessment. Even if there are, they must not be privately given or received. Two, a treaty was signed with Japanese Admiral Shiiozawa, agreeing that shells would not land on naval ships and that no shots would be fired. International treaties must be approved by the government and cannot be signed privately by any agency. Anyone with a little common sense can understand this. The so-called treaty between our army and Shiiozawa is said to be based on what? Three, the navy is corrupt on weekdays, and it is unspeakable. Our army has been working hard for years, day and night, and has been striving for various important government affairs and dare not slack off. All work has reports that can be verified. The member regards it as corruption and should be ordered to point out conclusive evidence. Four, the Marine Corps is not on the ships, but is planting opium in Fujian. The Marine Corps of all countries are not stationed on ships during peacetime. The member is ignorant of the navy's situation and the world situation, so he has this bizarre statement. Moreover, the Marine Corps stationed in Fujian has a good relationship with the local people, and the ban on smoking in the area where it is stationed has been repeatedly emphasized. The member fabricated slander without any evidence. The military's reputation is at stake, and all the soldiers are deeply indignant. Five, the useless navy should be completely abolished and the ships sold to merchants. The proceeds from the sale of the ships and the navy's expenses should be used to purchase 200 submarines to defend the sea. The configuration of warships and merchant ships is different, and it is difficult to apply the conversion of warships into merchant ships. As for the purchase cost of submarines, the small ones cost several million yuan per ship. If calculated at 200 ships, the cost is huge. Even if the cost of selling the warships and the navy's expenses are all allocated, how many ships can be purchased? The member has no naval common sense, and his plan is contrary to the facts. Moreover, the establishment of the navy by the country is not only responsible for defending the country during the war, but also for pacifying the rivers and seas and defending the local area in peacetime, which is an urgent task. In addition to submarines, should other ships be used to share the responsibility of patrolling and defending? Those who know the truth will be able to distinguish. The ships of our army have been working diligently to suppress bandits. As soon as they hear of bandit alarms, they rush to aid day and night. The details of what happened have been reported in detail and can be reviewed. The member said that he watched the pirates rampantly and had not heard of the navy having a plan to eliminate them. His reversal of black and white and arbitrary barking is even more hateful. The above items are based on the facts. Looking at the point of law again, according to Article 10 of the revised Impeachment Law promulgated by the National Government on June 25th of this year, Supervisory Yuan personnel shall not disclose any impeachment case to the outside world before it is transferred to the disciplinary agency, in order to protect the dignity of the council system and prevent the malpractices of lobbying. The member is responsible for the important task of supervision and should strictly abide by it, but he does not know how to check himself and has preemptively disclosed important cases, not only destroying the reputation of our army, but also violating the order and disregarding the regulations of the council. He is like this in one case, and it can be seen in other cases. Moreover, the member also said that Director Yu often said, why bother to use the blood, sweat, and money of the people of the country to maintain the rice bowls of the people of Fujian? Because the current navy has become the world of the hereditary Fujian people. According to the Nanjing Evening News of the 10th of this month, Director Yu said in Shanghai that the newspaper reported that Supervisory Committee member Gao You-tang made remarks in Jinan. According to Yu Youren, Gao said that the heads of various departments and ministries, 19 of them, have been impeached, which is not the case. What he said was that every time I went to the Central Government to attend a meeting, I looked around and saw that most of the people who had been impeached were glaring at me. It is baseless and does not need to be defended. As for the affairs of the Ministry of Navy, what is said is that why bother to use the blood, sweat, and money of the people of the country to maintain the rice bowls of the people of Fujian? It is the original text of a certain supervisory committee member impeaching the Minister of Navy. I thought at the time that the affairs of the Navy Department should not offend the people of Fujian Province. Therefore, I once told the original impeacher that the impeachment case should be based on facts and should not be a vague criticism. Now, the remarks are pointed to as my words, which is even more contrary to the facts. The other sections are mostly related to Gao Jun's personal feelings, and I naturally cannot answer on his behalf. It can be seen that the member's remarks are completely fabricated. With such important remarks, he has planted blame on the head of our agency. In addition to slandering our army, there are various arguments for insulting the government and alienating feelings. His intentions are even more unpredictable. Reputation is the second life of a soldier. If he is slandered for no reason, it is not appropriate to remain silent. In order to respect the authority of the government and maintain the regulatory rules of supervision, it is difficult to allow the member to privately confuse the situation. It is appropriate to present this to your hospital and ask you to forward it to the appropriate authorities for investigation and handling in accordance with the law, in order to uphold the order and maintain the military's reputation. I am extremely sincere and awaiting orders.]

E Province Government Convenes

Political Reorganization Conference

Chiang Kai-shek Summons County Magistrates to Urge Bandit Suppression

Members of Post-War Rehabilitation Committees in Various Counties Have Been Selected

Hankou Correspondence: Commander-in-Chief Chiang previously ordered the E Province Government to convene county magistrates to the provincial capital for a meeting, and scheduled a personal interview. A total of forty-five county magistrates came to the province upon summons. At 9:00 AM on the 12th, they were led by Provincial Chairman Xia Douyin, Civil Affairs Director Zhu Huai Bing (Bi Hui Kang acting), Finance Director Shen Zhao Nian, Education Director Shen Shi Yuan, Construction Director Li Shu Cheng, Committee Members Kong Geng, Yan Xunfu, Cheng Ru Huai, Secretary-General Yang Zaichun, etc., to the headquarters to meet Chiang. Chiang first summoned the magistrates of Yidu, Badong, and Mianyang counties, individually inquiring about local conditions. He then summoned the entire group for a speech, generally stating that banditry in E Province was rampant for many reasons, but the biggest problem was past inaction and perfunctoriness. The county is a unit of self-governance, and the magistrate is an official close to the people. It is a disgrace for a magistrate to sit by and watch the people be ravaged by bandits. From now on, each magistrate should redouble their efforts, be willing to sacrifice, and be responsible. They should organize the masses, use local self-defense forces, and cooperate with local fair-minded people to thoroughly eliminate banditry. Regarding counties with bandits, they must have a clear investigation and reorganization plan regarding the bandit situation, how to proceed with suppression, as well as local security conditions, and transportation construction status, etc. He also said that if military officers stationed in various places, from division commanders down, bully county magistrates, they are permitted to telegraph the headquarters for handling. After the speech, he personally instructed Xia Douyin to hold a local political reorganization conference in the provincial capital within three days, for a period of three days. The attendees were stipulated to be nine party and government committee members from the headquarters, ten provincial chairman, directors, committee members, and secretary-general, six secretaries and section chiefs from the civil, finance, and construction departments, four secretaries and section chiefs from the provincial secretariat, and forty-five county magistrates. Those who have not reported will join at any time. After receiving the order, Xia immediately sent out notifications on the evening of the 12th, scheduling the start of the meeting at 8:00 AM on the 13th, to be completed on the 15th. The conference will formulate detailed plans and reports on methods of bandit suppression, disaster relief, security, and construction in various counties, to be submitted to the headquarters for selection and implementation.

Furthermore, the provincial government received an order from Chiang to promptly select and recommend personnel for post-war rehabilitation in bandit areas and local gentry assisting in the suppression. Each county must guarantee the selection of two people, a head and a deputy. Every three or four counties will be designated as a post-war rehabilitation district, and two people will be guaranteed selection in each, with special privileges and respect, so that they can work hard for their hometowns and be responsible for assisting in the suppression. The civil affairs department was immediately ordered to compile a list and submit it to the headquarters for review on the 12th. It is planned that in the eastern E area, Qishui, Qichun, Luotian, and Guangji will be one district, with Committee Chairman Li Shiqiao and Committee Member Wen Juntian. Macheng, Huang'an, Huangpi, and Xiaogan will be one district, with Committee Chairman Cheng Ru Huai and Committee Member Yu Yu Zhi. In the central E area, Mianyang, Qianjiang, Jianli, and Hanyang will be one district, with Committee Chairman Nan Xian and Committee Member Ai Yu Ying. Hekou, Tianmen, Yingcheng, and Jingshan will be one district, with Committee Chairman Yan Xunfu and Committee Members Lu De Ze and Zuo Duo. In the southern E area, Yangxin, Daye, Echeng, Xianning, Tongshan, Chongyang, and Tongcheng will be one district, with Committee Chairman Yu Zi Xiang and Committee Member Wang Shi Liu. The county committee members are: Qishui Committee Member Li Shiqiao, Deputy Committee Member Guo Zhao, Qichun Committee Member Ling Shao Mei, Luotian Committee Member Liu Hong Yu, Deputy Committee Member Fang Guo Qing, Macheng Committee Member Zheng Mei Xuan, Deputy Committee Member Zheng Jie Qiao, Huang'an Committee Member Shi Yu Ling, Deputy Committee Member Chen Tie Hou, Huangpi Committee Member Li Xuan Xuan, Xiaogan Committee Member Jiang Shao Yuan, Deputy Committee Member Wang Bao He, Yangxin Committee Member Chen Zhi Ping, Daye Committee Member Liu Min Ru, Deputy Committee Member Tian Wei Zhong, Echeng Committee Member Hu Shun Sun, Deputy Committee Member Xia Lin Shu, Xianning Committee Member Yuan Qi Qing, Tongshan Committee Member Ruan Zheng Qing, Deputy Committee Member Xia Wen Ying, Chongyang Committee Member Rao Shu Fan, Deputy Committee Member Yu Tian, Tongcheng Committee Member Ge Song Chu, Deputy Committee Member Xia Feng Shi, Mianyang Committee Member Liu Shou Xin, Deputy Committee Member Yan Shuo, Qianjiang Committee Member Zhu Xin Fo, Deputy Committee Member Yuan Xuan Cheng, Jianli Committee Member Chuan Xiang Rong, Hanchuan Committee Member Chen Zong Kai, Deputy Committee Member Wang Zhen Nan, Tianmen Committee Member Hu Zi Ming, Deputy Committee Member Zeng Mao Tang, Yingcheng Committee Member Jiang Zuo Lin, Deputy Committee Member Zuo Duo, Jingshan Committee Member Liu Pei Qing, Deputy Committee Member Yin Shi Dao, Hanyang Committee Member Yan Jing, Deputy Committee Member Zhang Han Qing, Guangji Committee Member Zhou Wu Yi, Deputy Committee Member Gao Zhao Huang. (July 12th)

Local Dispatches

Songjiang

Changes in Educational Administration Personnel: Since the change of leadership in the county education bureau, the internal affairs have been greatly reorganized. It has recently been learned that the bureau received an order from the education department to dismiss supervisor Zhang Zhao Yun and replace him with Zhang Xing Xin. Committee members Shen Ru and Yan Zhen Bang have been dismissed, and replacements have not yet been announced. Previously, the elementary schools in the fourth district jointly presented a petition to retain the district education committee member. After being reprimanded by the bureau, the committee member, Xu Zong Yao, voluntarily resigned. The bureau approved the resignation and appointed Yin Xi Xiong as his replacement, who has reportedly gone to take over his duties.

The Aftermath of Cheng Jun's Being Torn: Cheng Jun, the former head of the public security bureau, was residing in Fengjing. When the Japanese invaders were rampant in the Shanghai area and the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Qiantang Railway was in a tense situation, Cheng immediately led his relatives, Ye Yisun, his wife and daughters, and hired a boat to seek refuge in Dongzha. On the way, they encountered a bandit boat that ordered them to stop and boarded the boat to rob them. Cheng was Ye's brother-in-law, and the two daughters were his nieces. The family was wealthy, and if they were kidnapped, it would be extremely dangerous. Therefore, he was mindful of his familial relations and stepped forward, instructing the bandits to release everyone else and leave him alone, so that they could raise money for his ransom. The bandits complied. Cheng Jun was thus kidnapped by the bandits. When Ye returned home, he kept it a secret. Even when Cheng's family inquired, he did not admit that they had been attacked by bandits and kidnapped. It was only after time had passed and Cheng had been killed that they learned the details. Cheng's family, in great pain, suspected Ye of colluding with the bandits and reported him to the Water Bandit Suppression Command, which detained Ye for interrogation. The case was deemed a matter of justice and transferred to Songjiang, where it is currently being investigated by the county court's prosecutor's office. He was interrogated again yesterday, and his testimony remained the same as before. It is unknown how this case will be resolved.

Suzhou

Four Major Bandits Transferred to Bandit Suppression Headquarters for Interrogation: The first district of the Water Public Security Bureau captured four Lake bandits in Shanghai: Zhang the Blind, Gao Ben Gen, Yun Zhou, and Zeng Pin Rong. Yesterday, they were transferred to the Suzhou-Songjiang Bandit Suppression Headquarters for interrogation. Bandit leader Zhang the Blind confessed to the Bandit Suppression Headquarters that he was from Anhui, his original name was Zhang Pu Yuan, and he served as a policeman in Zhejiang in the seventh year of the Republic [1918]. On February 17th of this year [1937], he colluded with Kong Xiang Hao, Wang Tu Zi, Ruan Li Yun, Xiao Ai, etc., and started a gang in Caojing, using the guise of selling salt to secretly rob. On March 3rd, in Shangmingdian, they kidnapped a Linghu man named Zhang. Later, they joined a gang to rob the Suzhou-bound passenger ship. Wang Yu Shan, a military officer from the 19th Army Transportation Department, was shot and killed by Gu Xing Wen. Later, they encountered police fire at Dianshan Lake. The next day, they encountered police fire twice more in Zhou Zhuang, resulting in many casualties on their side. He jumped into the water and escaped, and was sent to Shanghai from Fengjing. Their guns were all taken away by Qin Xiu Zi. On June 19th, a monk named Zhou invited him to go to Shan to commit a crime, arranging to meet on June 30th. Unexpectedly, he was arrested that morning. He continued to interrogate the other three bandits, then ordered them to be detained pending investigation.

Guerrilla Soldiers Make a Ruckus at the Theater: The Suzhou Grand Theater in the northern district of Suzhou was showing a film at 9:00 PM on the 12th when suddenly more than ten water police guerrilla soldiers, each holding iron rulers and bayonets, stormed in through the front door and rushed into the accounting room. They cut the telephone lines, smashed more than twenty pieces of glass from the large glass windows, and destroyed advertising lights, etc., and then roared away. It is reported that the losses amounted to over a thousand yuan.

Wuxi

Local Silk Factories Still Able to Sell Well: The silk factories in this county have been successively shutting down due to the dire silk market and sluggish foreign sales, resulting in huge losses and even bankruptcy. Now, a few factories are continuing to operate to maintain the livelihood of their workers. Fortunately, domestic silk sales have been brisk recently. In May of this year, Suzhou silk factories purchased twenty pieces of You Yong brand silk from the Taifeng silk factory in this county, valued at 585 taels; five pieces of Que Que brand, valued at 550 taels; five pieces of Tiao Wu brand and ten pieces of Song Bai brand from the Qian Shen silk factory, valued at 550 taels; ten pieces of Er Quan brand, valued at 530 taels; ten pieces of Di Qiu brand from Yongtai, valued at 52 taels; and ten pieces of Di Qiu brand, valued at 500 taels. The Huafeng silk factory in Huzhou also purchased ten pieces of Song Bai brand from Ding Chang, valued at 550 taels, and ten pieces of Huang Pai brand from Yuan Kang, valued at 490 taels. In July, the Suzhou silk factory purchased five pieces from Yufeng, valued at 530 taels; five pieces from Yuji, valued at 580 taels; and five pieces of Jin Ma brand from Ji Ji, valued at 470 taels. In the months of May, June and July, a total of 120 pieces of factory silk were sold, with Huzhou being the strongest market, purchasing 60 pieces in June, followed by Suzhou.

Changzhou

Kidnapping Case Occurs in the Eighth District: Xie Bing Rong's home in Dongxin Township, the eighth district of Wu County, was suddenly attacked by more than ten bandits a few days ago, who wantonly searched and looted. Not satisfied, they also kidnapped Xie's sixteen-year-old son, Yuan Kang, and left a note demanding a ransom of 35,000 yuan, instructing them to contact them in Nanjing within seven days. Afterwards, the chief of the eighth sub-bureau of public security in charge of the area reported the case to the county on the 12th, requesting an arrest.

Gaoyou

Hurricane Causes Disaster in Mapengwan: Mapengwan Town, located thirty li north of Youcheng on the canal levee, is an important transportation hub between north and south. Although the town is small in area, commerce is fairly developed. The town has a population of 112 families, less than a thousand people, mostly engaged in business and quite wealthy. Unexpectedly, at about 8:00 PM on the 9th of this month, there was a sudden storm of wind and rain, with particularly violent winds, lasting for more than ten minutes before stopping. In an instant, an unprecedented disaster occurred. At the southern end of the town, there is Taiping Lane. When the hurricane first started, it began in the middle of the lane and continued to the rice mill at the northern end of the town. All the shops and houses were destroyed, leaving only six buildings, including the rice mill at the north end of the town. Countless trees in the town were destroyed, and two utility poles were also snapped. Most tragically, at the Zhao Da Fang Inn in the town, there were two male and female travelers dressed as students who were staying at the inn that night. They were both killed in the disaster. The heads and abdomens of the man and woman were crushed by bricks and tiles, a bloody mess. Also, a tugboat docked in the town's canal, with seven or eight canal workers sleeping in the cabin, was swept into the air by the hurricane. When the wind stopped, it overturned in the river, drowning five people, one of whom had his abdomen ruptured and his intestines spilling out, a tragic sight. The others were all seriously injured. Three or four small boats in the canal were also overturned by the hurricane, drowning Wang and Wanfu Gui. The others were rescued. There were many civilian casualties in the town, but no accurate count is yet available. It is reported that the losses are estimated at 200,000 to 300,000 yuan. The essence of the town has been destroyed, truly an unprecedented catastrophe. It is also reported that in Maojiazhuang near the town, more than ten houses were destroyed by the wind that night, but fortunately no one was injured.

Jiaxing

Large Number of Robbers Sentenced Separately: Farmers Lin Yi Mao in Baofu Township, Wangdian District, Jiaxing, and the Gao family in Xing were robbed one after another, and the owners were stabbed. The Baofu Township Defense Corps discovered the bandits' trail and, together with the district defense corps and the water police, cracked the bandit gang, arresting the criminals Gao Ming Yuan, Fan Xiu Song, Chen Ming Yuan, Chen Xiao Gao Zi, Chen Ge Shi, Chen Tou Zi, and Fan Wang Shi. They were sent to court for interrogation. The Jiaxing County Public Security Bureau's Criminal Investigation Team also captured two fugitive criminals, Gao Tian Yuan and Shen Wen, in Jiaxing and sent them to the court. The court ordered the owners to appear in court to clearly identify them. Yesterday, the court sentenced the main criminals, Gao Tian Yuan, Gao Ming Yuan, Fan Xiu Song, Chen Ming Yuan, and Chen Xiao Gao Zi, to eight years in prison and eight years of deprivation of civil rights. Shen Wen was sentenced to seven years in prison and seven years of deprivation of civil rights. Chen Ge Shi was sentenced to two years in prison. Fan Wang Shi was sentenced to three months. Chen Tou Zi was exempted from prosecution because he was under twelve years old. The other three bandits, Chen Da Zi, Zhou Qi, and Chen Lao San, who are still at large, will be tried separately when they are arrested.

Bandit Kidnapping Organization Cracked in Yu Xian District: On the afternoon of the 11th, members of the Yu Xian Town Sixth District Basic Team detained a suspect named Zhou Chang Ming in front of the Tian Sheng Chang cigarette shop in the western market of the town. He was taken to the team headquarters and interrogated by the Sixth District Chief and Team Leader, who revealed that Chen Ren Guan, who lived in the Da Cao Wang Temple area about three li from the town, had recently sent a letter to Huang Ting Rui, the town chief of You Guang Da Qiao Town, threatening him and demanding a loan of 3,000 yuan, using the alias Yi Shi Bin, and instructing him to reply within three days and have the letter delivered to the Tian Sheng Chang cigarette shop in Yu Xian Town. Zhou was arrested while Chen Ren Guan ordered him to pick up the letter at the shop. The team members then went to Da Cao Wang Temple to arrest Chen, but Chen had fled. Only the landlord, Li Sheng Shi, was apprehended. Chen Ren Guan's biological father, Chen Liang Bing, and his wife, Wu Shi, were arrested in the Tangxi area on the afternoon of the 11th. Wu A Biao, the father of Chen's wife Wu, was apprehended in Da Qiao Town (Wu is a major suspect). On the afternoon of the 12th, the team sent all the arrested persons to the Jiaxing branch court for interrogation.

Full Funding to Be Issued Starting in July

丨Wang Jingwei Replies to National Schools丨

Wang Jingwei replied to the presidents of national universities, college presidents, and vocational school presidents, saying that he fully understands the importance of educational funding. Conference of Presidents of Vocational Schools and Above

Discussing Funding Issues

Solutions Have Been Found

Nanjing, 13th: The conference of presidents of national vocational schools and above has been discussing issues for several days, with funding being the center of all other issues. In addition to submitting three points to the Central Political Conference and the Executive Yuan: (1) Funding for national colleges and universities will be issued in full starting in July. (2) A method for definitively clearing up the arrears of the previous year should be determined, either by paying cash in installments or issuing bonds with reliable collateral. (3) Funding for national colleges and universities should be designated to guarantee it, such as: A. Organizing a Central Education and Culture Funding Management Committee to manage it. B. Designating the following funds: 1. Customs duties, 2. Russian Boxer Indemnity and others, 3. Funds allocated by the Railway Department to the Ministry of Finance, 4. Cigarette special tax. The designated funds should be directly allocated monthly by the special collection agencies to the aforementioned Management Committee. A summary of the resolutions is as follows: 1. Delete the words "may be divided into two departments" from Item 2 of Article 5 of the University Organization Law, and add Item 3 to the same article: "Schools that teach art and music, if their programs are equivalent to university programs, may also be called independent colleges." 2. Important agriculture, engineering, medical, and science colleges, and national universities located in the same area should avoid duplication of departments, with the principle of enriching the content of the schools. The above-mentioned colleges may be re-established depending on the financial situation. Universities should cultivate talent for national defense construction, and the Ministry of Education should investigate the departments established by each school and the subjects they are good at researching to cultivate talent separately.

Measures for Overseas Students to Return to China for Further Education

Nanjing, 13th: The Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission has stipulated that overseas students returning to China for further education and requesting recommendation or introduction by the Commission must have a certificate or letter of introduction from the local national consulate, party headquarters, chamber of commerce, or a cultural institution registered with the Commission. In special circumstances where it is not possible to complete the aforementioned procedures, a member of the Commission may be responsible for certification and submit a graduation diploma, study certificate, transfer certificate, school transcript, etc. Those who genuinely have financial difficulties and request free education must have a reliable certificate from the local national consulate, senior party headquarters, chamber of commerce, or a cultural institution registered with the Commission.

The British Boxer Indemnity and Cultural Undertakings

(I)

Secretary-General Hang of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board Announces the Situation, Guowenshe: Recently, financial difficulties in the educational sector have left them with no solutions. They all hope that the management of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board will provide assistance, but the Board has no way to provide relief, which it fears will not be understood. Therefore, Secretary-General Hang Liwu announced his personal situation as follows: After the United States took the lead in returning a portion of the Boxer Indemnity to establish Tsinghua University, all countries have taken returning the Boxer Indemnity to carry out education and cultural undertakings as their aim. In the winter of the eleventh year of the Republic [1922], the British government declared that "[the outstanding Boxer Indemnity payable by China will be returned to China for use in educational and cultural undertakings beneficial to both countries]." Later, due to the general election in the British Parliament and successive changes in the cabinet, it was shelved. It was not until June of the fourteenth year of the Republic [1925] that the British Parliament officially passed [the Chinese Indemnity Bill], which was confirmed as necessary to study the use in advance. A consultative committee was established, consisting of eleven members, eight British and three Chinese (Mr. Hu Shi, Mr. Ding Wenjiang, and Mr. Wang Jingchun). In the fifteenth year of the Republic [1926], the committee organized a delegation to China to investigate and solicit opinions on the use of the returned indemnity. In the same year, the delegation prepared a report. Afterwards, China and Britain exchanged notes, which became the basis. Therefore, on September 19th of the nineteenth year of the Republic [1930], the first exchange of notes on the Sino-British Indemnity was resolved. In the first paragraph of Minister Wang's note to British Minister Lampson, it states, "[The Minister deeply hopes that your government will hand over to the Chinese government for management the full amount of the indemnity payable from December 1, 1922. After the actual handover of this money, the Chinese government intends to refer to the general intent of the report of the Sino-British Advisory Committee of 1926 for the handling of the money. The general intent of the report should be noted by the following board of directors. However, the Chinese government believes that the most beneficial plan for establishing a foundation in the first step is to reorganize and build Chinese railways and invest in other Chinese productive enterprises with most of the indemnity, namely, the current stored funds and future payable funds]." Furthermore, in the final paragraph of the same document, "[For the loans paid by the railways or other productive enterprises, interest should be paid and ultimately guaranteed. All funds for repaying the principal and interest of the loans should be handed over to the board of directors, which will immediately use them for educational undertakings]." Subsequently, the second plenary meeting of the Central Committee in May of the eighteenth year of the Republic [1929], and the 226th meeting in May of the nineteenth year of the Republic [1930] and the 262nd political meeting on February 25th of the following year [1931], resolved that the methods for allocating the indemnity and the principles for guaranteeing interest should all be in accordance with the exchange of notes and clearly stipulated. It is estimated that the Ministry of Railways will be able to borrow two-thirds of the entire British Boxer Indemnity, the Huai River Waterways Commission will be able to borrow 40% of one-third of the entire British Boxer Indemnity, the Guangdong River Management Committee will be able to borrow 20% of one-third of the entire British Boxer Indemnity, and the Construction Committee, the Ministry of Industry, and the Yellow River Water Conservancy Committee will each be able to borrow one-third of 40% of one-third of the entire British Boxer Indemnity.

Disturbance at the Chinese Public School

Yesterday's Open House: Students Refused to Pick Up Scraps of Paper and Fruit Peels

British Teacher Slaps Student: Ordered to Leave the School

At the Chinese Public School at 63 Haskell Road, an open house was held yesterday afternoon at 4:30 PM. About seven or eight hundred students and parents attended. When the parents were having tea and snacks, scraps of paper and fruit peels were scattered all over the ground. A British teacher (Anslice) then ordered the student Hong Zu Xiu (a student in the second B class of junior high school) to pick them up from the ground. Hong refused because cleaning up the venue was the responsibility of the school staff. The teacher slapped Hong with his hand and dragged him to the classroom on the second floor, where he punched him in the face and other places. All the students in the third year of junior high school witnessed this and were extremely angry. They expressed a common opinion, and together with the parents present, led by Hong Zu Xiu's father, they negotiated with the principal. Unexpectedly, Principal J. Moffat sided with the teacher, saying that the student had disobeyed orders and deserved to be punished. At that time, He Sheng Chang, a student in the third year of junior high school, spoke passionately and argued reasonably, but the principal, running out of arguments, turned red and became angry with He Sheng Chang, grabbing him, slapping him several times, and immediately expelling all the students and parents from the school, sealing the school gate.

Wang Jiyuan

War Zone Relics Painting Exhibition Closes Tonight

After the Japanese troops withdrew, the famous painter Wang Jiyuan repeatedly went to the war zones of Wusong, Jiangwan, Miaohang, and Nanxiang, and painted dozens of works, using his newly created Chinese brushwork and Western colors, and carefully mounted them into scrolls using ancient Chinese methods. Since the 9th of this month, they have been displayed for six days at 90 Marcel Thirot Road, the intersection of Luban Road. Hundreds of people visit every day. The Past and Present of the World Games

(9)

(8) Review of Past Field and Track Competitions (Middle)

Fifth Session Although the aforementioned sessions were not yet free from their initial stages, the truly worthy World Olympic Games began with the fifth session in London, England, in 1908. The number of events increased to twenty-three, and most of the events set new records. The astonishing performances of Canada, South Africa, and Sweden added greatly to the spectacle of the Games. The United States experienced its first losses in the 100-meter and 200-meter races. American athletes won only the 800-meter, 1500-meter, marathon, high hurdle, and intermediate hurdle events. 巴特's time of one minute and 52.8 seconds in the 800-meter race remained unbroken for a long time, until it was surpassed by German doctor 貝爾則 at Stanford Bridge in 1926. The consecutive victories of 弗浪那根 in the hammer throw event are also noteworthy. At the closing of the session, the United States remained the champion, but the outstanding performance of British athletes marked the first time they had posed a serious challenge to the American athletes.

Sixth Session The session was held in Stockholm, the capital of Sweden, in 1912. The solemn and magnificent opening ceremony was unprecedented. The results of the Games produced numerous new world records. The outstanding performances of 克雷 (USA) in the 100-meter and 200-meter races, 茂雷迪斯 (USA) in the 800-meter race, 傑克遜 (England) in the 1500-meter race, and 枸爾梅尼 (Finland) in the 5000-meter and 10000-meter races were truly remarkable. These are just a few examples from the track events. In the field events, the long jump was just under 25 feet, the pole vault was nearly 13 feet, the javelin throw reached approximately 200 feet, the discus throw was around 150 feet, and the shot put exceeded 50 feet. Only four records from 1908 remained unbroken. With the continued dominance of the United States and the emergence of strong athletes from countries such as Finland and Sweden, the World Olympic Games reached a new level of competitiveness. Enthusiasts believed that the next session in 1916 would produce even more incredible results.

During the European War Unexpectedly, misfortune struck. The outbreak of the war prevented athletes from competing in track and field events. Instead, they went to the battlefield. The seventh Olympic Games, originally scheduled to be held in Berlin, Germany, in 1916, was destroyed by the ashes of the European War.

Seventh Session After the European War, the small European countries suffered deeply and began to actively promote sports to strengthen the physical fitness of their citizens. At the seventh session in 1920, which was restored in Antwerp, the capital of Belgium, Finnish athletes emerged as a new force, creating a special situation in the World Olympic Games. At the same time, the impact of the war caused some athletes to fall behind, resulting in a balanced situation with advances and setbacks. In the intense competition, the pole vault reached a new world record of 4.09 meters, and the javelin throw reached 65.78 meters. The time of 14.8 seconds in the 110-meter hurdles by 加拿大托姆遜 was particularly shocking. Notably, the veteran hero 芬蘭柯爾梅尼 returned and won the marathon, shortening the previous record by thirteen seconds. 芬蘭納米 made his debut at the event, winning the 5000-meter and 10000-meter cross-country races. He later set world records in events ranging from one mile to five miles as easily as reaching into his pocket.

Page 11

Free Talk

Poetic Prophecy

Strange! Du Mu, a poet of the Tang Dynasty, was actually a prophet! His abilities were similar to those of Li Chunfeng and Liu Bowen; his "Autumn Evening" poem also possessed the same mystery as the "Tui Bei Tu" and the "Shaobing Song"!

"Silver candles in the autumn night cast a cold light on the painted screen, a small silk fan brushes away fireflies; the steps of heaven are cold as water in the night, I lie and watch the Cowherd and Weaver Girl stars." Isn't this poem familiar to everyone? It's simply thought to be about an autumn evening in the Tang Dynasty! Who knew it would instead be about an autumn evening in Beiping in the 21st year of the Republic [1932], composed out of a sense of indignation towards the Beiping authorities' large-scale arrest of movie stars.

Movie stars rely entirely on excitement on the silver screen; now, they've become silver candles casting a cold light on the painted screen. The silver screen is desolate; one can imagine the scene. This is the first line of the poetic prophecy.

What are fireflies? Of course, they're stars. In ancient poetry, fireflies are always compared to stars; lines like "soaring in the sky like stars" and "scattered like stars, wanting to approach the moon before the railings" are proof of this. Du Mu's "a small silk fan brushes away fireflies" refers to the large-scale arrest of movie stars. The "罗" [luo, silk] in "轻罗" [qing lu, light silk] is borrowed to reflect the "罗" [luo, net] in "罗网" [luo wang, net]. A large number of movie stars were easily caught in the net; it truly was a case of "a small silk fan brushes away fireflies". This is the second line of the poetic prophecy.

Beiping was the capital of past emperors; the phrase "天阶" [tian jie, steps of heaven] likely refers to the heavenly prison. The character "阶" [jie, steps] means "prisoner in the dungeon". Male and female movie stars were arrested together; male stars are naturally the Cowherd, and female stars are naturally the Weaver Girl. In the dungeon, the autumn is cool as water; how pitiful it is to see these male and female stars lying inside! This is the prophecy of the third and fourth lines.

How wondrous and strange; Mr. Du Mu can become sworn brothers with Chunfeng and Bowen, becoming a trio among the prophets.

A Narration on the Origin of Pork Floss

— Bicheng

One day, I took a steamer from Anting to Taicang. There were two people on the boat, speaking the Taicang dialect. They brought out wine and drank together, accompanied by Taicang-style pork floss. They drank and talked with relish. A guest asked about the popularity of pork floss. They said that it originated with Ni Hongshun of Taicang. Even in the vast commercial port of Shanghai today, sellers of pork floss still display Ni Hongshun's old brand. Just like the soy duck and soy meat of Lao Sanzhen and Lu Gaojian, using this brand is necessary to show high quality. Is it the same for Ni Hongshun's pork floss? One of the drinkers stopped his cup and replied, "Indeed. However, Ni Hongshun was not the originator of pork floss. In fact, it was created by a prominent official with a reputation in politics. Who was this person? It was none other than Qian Tiaofu, Minister Qian Dingming of Taicang." During the early years of Tongzhi, when Suzhou and Changzhou fell to the rebels, Qian Gong, as a licentiate representative of the Suzhou, Songjiang, and Taicang prefectures, requested troops from Governor-General Zeng. Governor-General Zeng then dispatched Li Hongzhang to lead troops from Shanghai, thereby pacifying the various prefectures. Qian Gong also abandoned his pen and joined the military. Later, he became Governor of Hunan. It is said that at that time, the cooks in the Governor's residence were highly skilled at seasoning and were good at creating new foods, not sticking to old methods. It is a pity that they did not emulate the Old Man of Suiyuan and write a cookbook to benefit the elderly. However, even this one dish of pork floss has brought great fame to Taicang and greatly benefited the Ni family, a result that cannot be considered unadmirable. According to the method of making pork floss, there is a special secret. It is said that snake oil must be used to prevent spoilage over time. Stored in containers, there is no need to remove the air, which is comparable to today's canned food. Even more strange is that the use of snake oil repels mosquitoes and flies. Based on this principle, microorganisms may not easily grow within it. As for the deliciousness of the flavor, it is also due to the use of snake oil. It is said that when Qian Gong retired to private life, he often made pork floss to entertain guests. It was made by Hongshun, who had served Gong in Hunan for a long time and had a good understanding of cooking. When Gong returned, he taught him the method of making pork floss. After Gong's death, Hongshun used his skills to set up a pork floss stall. He used his own name to print paper for the brand. After more than a year, he accumulated some capital and rented a house to set up a shop. Year after year, business prospered. Today, stores are opened in major cities, run by his children and grandchildren. However, it is no longer known whether snake oil is still used. Although Taicang is the place of origin, it is not closely studied today. However, the three characters 'Ni Hongshun' are still used as a brand to attract customers. In the future, they may even use phrases such as 'The First House' as a necessary trend. The guest listened and nodded. I then wrote it down for the compilation of local history."

Peculiar Production Methods

— Binlang

Recently, a friend wrote from Moscow, mentioning that since the implementation of the Second Five-Year Plan in Russia, the entire country, regardless of gender, has been dedicated to their respective roles, striving to advance the cause of production. This spirit of diligence and thrift is worthy of admiration. He said that in Soviet Russia, not even a blade of grass or a handful of soil is easily discarded. All potential industrial raw materials are sought everywhere with meticulous attention. For example, the recent research and utilization of "dog hair" is also worthy of note. The authorities have counted the total number of "dogs" in the country, estimating it at twenty-five million. These many dogs can supply two thousand tons of dog hair annually. Such a huge amount of dog hair provides considerable support to the wool industry in the Five-Year Plan. Therefore, a nationwide order has been issued, urging people to shear dog hair and sell it at a price. The general idea is: "In general, livestock with long hair suffer from increased heat and constant panting in the summer. Dogs are beneficial domestic animals to humans. Their hair should be sheared and sold at a price. Not only is it beneficial to the dog's hygiene, but it can also significantly increase the output of industrial raw materials." As a result, almost all shorn dogs can be seen throughout Russia. Naturally, the increase in dog hair is not small. That kind of production method is truly groundbreaking.

About Women

— Liusha

Euphemisms for menstruation are avoided by most women, who replace them with various different terms. According to Xu Ou, "[Among the Latin and Teutonic peoples, the term 'menstruation' is commonly replaced with the equivalent term 'flowers,' because flowers symbolize the possibility of fruition.]" According to Du De, "[Some uncivilized tribes refer to menstruation as 'wearing deerskin' or 'going out'.]"

German women use the idiom "[I have mail again]" or "[Aunt has arrived]" when menstruating. Chinese women say "[The body has come]" or "[The mother-in-law has come]". However, Chinese female students often use "Menses" or "Bad Days" as substitutes.

Women's Pants In ancient China, women not only wore pants during the day but also refused to take them off when sleeping at night, and the pants of so-called upper-class women were tied even tighter when sleeping. However, the situation is quite different in the West. Originally, pants were Eastern clothing and seemed to have spread to Europe from Venice. Those who first adopted them in Europe were mostly prostitutes. It is said that if someone asked a peasant girl if she wore pants, she would exclaim, "[Would I wear pants? Madam! I am a respectable girl!]" According to a book published by Muir in 1783, Parisian women, except for actresses, did not wear pants. Of course, this trend has changed now.

Short News Poet Zhang Xiaojing is willing to befriend ink-lovers and write on fans. The ink fee is half a yuan per piece, and the deadline for pickup is three days. He also collaborates with Yin Junzhi'an to write on palm-leaf fans. The cost is low. Submissions can be sent to Duoyunxuan Fan Shop, Henan Road, or Choushijiao Art Society, No. 22, Yuqing Lane, Gordon Road.

The Xu family of Hejiang, Qingpu, has produced poets for generations, especially Xu Yusun, who has dominated the literary scene in the seven counties of Songqing for thirty years. In his later years, he set up a school in Liantang and wrote the "Bilian Ju Poetry Collection," which is fresh and elegant, directly following the style of the High Tang Dynasty. It has recently been published by his grandson and students for dissemination. If you wish to obtain a copy, it is said that each volume only costs three dimes for the paper. Postage stamps can be used as payment. Send a letter to Xu Lianfang, Legal Society, Dadong Bookstore, No. 2, North Fujian Road, Shanghai, and it will be sent immediately.

Random Talks by Di Xiangqi

— Gan

Zheng Xiaoxu

Zheng Xiaoxu's reputation does not come from his calligraphy or poetry initially. The world uniquely calls him a master of calligraphy and poetry. This is true. But in the rise and fall of Qing Dynasty politics, he often planned and was in fact a politician. He passed the provincial examination in the Renwu year and became a secretary in the central government. Ashamed to be a low-ranking official, he had the intention to leave. He told people, "Serving as an official and holding a low rank, one must cater to superiors every day. One can still have enough to eat and be warm outside, but those who live inside are so poor that they cannot support themselves. I do not want to stay in this position for long." So he left. Later he changed to office in Jiangsu. After that, he was stationed in Kobe as consul. Zheng Xiaoxu's interactions with Japanese people began at this time. Governor Zhang Zhidong heard his name and recruited him into his staff. He also submitted a memorial praising his talent as capable of great use, and he was granted the rank of Daotai. At that time, officials in Hubei often referred to him as Chief Secretary Zheng. His influence was evident. Zhidong had a long-standing relationship with Wang Renkan (Kezhuang)'s several sons. One of them was appointed to the province as a sub-prefect and wanted to join the governor's staff. He asked Liang Jie'an (Dingfen) to speak on his behalf to Zhidong. Zhidong remained silent. He persisted in his request and was scolded angrily. He desperately sought advancement. Unable to obtain his request, he would not give up. He once told Dingfen about this matter. Dingfen said, "It will definitely be reported." There was an errand to the Governor, and he spoke as before. Xiaoxu happened to be present. Zhidong, waited until he finished speaking, and said angrily, "My staff doesn't need talented people. Someone like that may not be able to do it." "You are in charge of the Lianghu Academy. How about bringing him in as an assistant to treat people and manage affairs?" Dingfen agreed. Xiaoxu said, "I do not think so. In the world, whose writing is better than yours, teacher? In the world, whose official documents are better than yours? It is easy to be a secretary for others, but difficult to be a secretary for a master. Precisely because it is difficult, someone must want it. They will seek knowledge from it. Kezhuang is a talented scholar. His son must be a mediocre person. We must investigate." He looked at Dingfen. Dingfen said, "Su is very eloquent and truly understands my heart. I wanted to say it but dared not speak." Zhidong smiled and said, "Su is eloquent but sarcastic. Jie'an also has a hidden meaning. If I don't agree, both of you will be unhappy. If I agree, I should try him with something. Allow me to scrutinize it carefully." In less than five days, the order came. People like to praise and denigrate. How could Zhidong not do so? Xiaoxu was good at words, so he achieved what Dingfen had repeatedly failed to do in a few words. He was truly understanding.

Records of Striking the Bell in the Ancient Temple

(50)

— Bu Chu Ting Cao Qifu

Fifty-five

Mr. Zhu believes that in this martial environment, it would be best for children to take a course in martial arts first, learning to be a little soldier. He suggested teaching the children some boxing techniques. This would be easy to arrange. Although Master Zhang had only been teaching for a short time, he had already found more than a dozen very promising disciples. They also wanted to drag me in as a children's boxing instructor. These dozen or so of us would be sufficient for distribution, and Master Zhang would not have to trouble himself. Just imagine how impressive it would be to see those little fists swinging around on the grass, witnessed by relatives and friends!

Fifty-six

"The children are here to study, how can they always be boxing?" Some ignorant people might say this. Mr. Zhu and I had anticipated this point. Just as he was calling me to have the students come read and learn characters, I was about to make a suggestion to him. I knew that my views were correct, and I was very happy. These are the texts that Mr. Zhu himself wrote.

(1)

Little soldier,

Don't underestimate.

If you bully China,

I'll fight you to the death.

(2)

Little soldier,

Loves to fight injustice.

We've risen up,

No need to recruit soldiers anymore.

(3)

Little soldier!

Ask: "What do you want to learn?"

"No one else wants to learn,

But I want to learn Yue Fei!"

Interest Rate Skyrockets

The recent surge in foreign interest rates has been spurred by the clamor for converting to a foreign currency standard. Banks, preparing for this change, have been competing to purchase foreign currency, resulting in a gradual increase in rates. Yesterday saw a particularly dramatic rise, with rates soaring by roughly three percent compared to the previous day. The silver interest rate, influenced by foreign banks absorbing cash, has also caused a squeeze in the market's active capital, leading to a sudden surge in overnight rates. This exceptional fluctuation is unprecedented for the summer season and marks a first for the year.

The Rise in Interest Rates is Dramatic. [Foreign Interest] The early morning interest rate was 6 qian, 9 fen, 8 li, an increase of 2 li, 8 hao, and 7 hu and a half compared to the early morning rate of the previous day. Industry insiders said that the Finance Ministry had approved a remission of one half of the tax differences for Dutch sugar ordered in February and March, causing buyers to disappear, and the market weakened. There were no purchases. Taikoo sugar prices were, B -16 taels and 3 qian, DY -15 taels and 5 qian and 5 fen, CW -15 taels and 8 qian, trade was weak and prices were settling.

To save Dutch sugar from collapse, the industry is planning to sell rough and white sugar publically. It’s rumored that internal arrangements are nearly done. A general industry meeting will be held to discuss the decision.

Silk and Tea: Foreign Firms' Silk Sales Still Lacking Vitality

European and American markets continue to weaken on Chinese silk prices; telegram transactions are sparse. Chinese silk merchants face significant losses from unsold stock. Domestic silk factories are also struggling due to the low-priced Japanese silk eroding sales. Market sentiment remains weak. Yesterday, only Dachang advanced with a Class B shipment of 13-15 bundles of Shanghai white factory silk, priced at only 520 taels. Samsung and others advanced with 15 bundles of second-grade yellow coarse silk, priced from 320 to 285 taels.

Tea Firms Enjoy Brisk European Sales of High-Quality Mei Tea

Yesterday, major British firms such as Xiehe, Yihua, and Jinjiang received substantial orders from Morocco for high-quality Mei green tea from Wudong, Tunxi, and other regions. They have begun large-scale procurement. Other traders are also taking advantage of the opportunity to purchase. Total transactions for Mei tea reached over 3,000 cases citywide. Transactions for Zhen Mei and Zhu tea of various grades are also trending upward. The long-depressed green tea market is showing signs of improvement. High-grade Qimen black tea is seeing increased activity, but the market for medium and low-grade tea remains sluggish.

Textiles

Nirong Sales Only Slightly Improved by the Dachuan Group

During this season, nirong (woolen fabric) transactions are weak. Yesterday, only the Dachuan group within the Dachuan Tong, Taikoo Yu, and Yihua Yu firms saw slight improvement. Plaid, solid color, and iridescent "Huade" nirong continued to be sold, but shipments were generally slow. Although the exchange rate shrank by 20 taels yesterday, it still required 260-270 taels per 1,000 taels, making it difficult to remit silver to Shanghai. Shanghai traders are advocating for shipments after prices fall. Aside from the Dachuan group, other small Sichuan groups from the Guandong, North China, and Yangtze River regions have shown no interest.

Metals: Pig Lead Price Falls to 36 Yuan

The overseas price of pig lead has plummeted. Yesterday's telegram indicated a price of only 36 gold yuan per ton, the lowest in decades. (This translates to only 10 taels in the Shanghai market, including all external expenses.) Consequently, the local market has been severely affected, with the standard price falling from 12 taels and 2.5 qian to 11 taels and 5 qian. However, with the current hot weather, sales are exceptionally slow, and the outlook is quite pessimistic.

Soviet Russia Procures Military Hardware

The metal market is sluggish due to the continuous hot weather. Besides minor transactions from a few factories, there are very few large-scale deals. However, yesterday saw a sudden surge in activity from the Soviet Russian authorities, who are urgently procuring a large quantity of military hardware in Shanghai, totaling over 4,000 dan. The purchased items include over 1,200 dan of #12 new lead wire, driving up the price by several qian. The market price rose from 9 taels and 5 qian to 10 taels and 2.5 qian. It is reported that the cargo arriving at the six banks in a week has also been purchased at a price of 9 taels and 8 or 9 qian. The current spot market is almost completely depleted. Over 500 bundles of "Huayuan" lead wire were offered at a price of 5 taels. Transactions also occurred for Three-Sheet black iron, thick steel plates, and tinplate, but their prices did not fluctuate much. In addition, there were inquiries for pig lead, copper, and pure antimony, but no firm deals were made.
