Re-examination of Russian Beggar's Corpse

No Injuries Found

Joint Examination by Renowned British and French Doctors

Brother of the Deceased Signs for and Claims Coffin

The suspicious death of Russian beggar Georgie Radikeff in the detention center of the Second Special District Court was re-examined yesterday morning at 10:00 AM at the body examination facility of the Shanghai Municipal Council Hospital on Dallas Road. The details are as follows:

Hiring Renowned British and French Doctors: Out of caution, the court, through the Chief Justice Ying Shi, instructed the forensic doctor Wei Ligong to invite renowned Shanghai forensic doctors to the scene for examination to ensure impartiality. Dr. Wei recommended Dr. Smith, the Commissioner of Health and Superintendent of the Hospital of the Shanghai Municipal Council, and French forensic doctor Dr. Villie, and Chief Justice Ying personally invited them. The two doctors arrived on time at 9:30 AM yesterday.

Personnel Present: Chief Justice Ying Shi, Criminal Court President Wang Wangxu, along with Head Clerk Xiao Jinfang, Clerk Zhu Chengzhuo, Accounting Section Head Clerk Wei Yuwei, interpreters Zhang Dengqu, Dong Chang, Zhang Qingchun, forensic doctors Wei Ligong, Jiang Xuan, also arrived successively. From the Police Department were Western Detective Sa Cai'er, fingerprinting and photography section chief Yu Ai'tuo, translator Xu Fengshu, lawyer Fei Xizhen, Shanghai Municipal Council Legal Advisor Dou Ge, and the Police Department-hired forensic doctor Shandelei. The plaintiff, the deceased’s brother Simon Greyteke, along with his attorney Pu Laimei, also arrived.

Head and Face Skin Completely Decomposed: After all personnel gathered, the Tongren Fu Yuan Funeral Home was notified by telephone to send the collection director Zhang Yunsheng with the funeral workers Zhu Bingsheng, Yang Jinquan, and Li Guisheng to the scene. The coffin was removed from the cold storage, and the seal affixed by Tongren Fu Yuan Funeral Home was inspected by the personnel present. The coffin was then carried to the autopsy room in the back. Upon opening the coffin, the body was found to be decomposed, with the skin on the head and face completely decomposed.

No Wounds on Upper or Lower Body: The body was then placed on the autopsy table, and the coffin sides were removed. Forensic doctor Wei Ligong began the examination with Jiang Xuan recording the details. The three British and French doctors jointly examined the body. Police Department doctor Shandelei asked the deceased’s brother Simon Greyteke if he recognized the body. Simon replied that his brother was missing two teeth on the lower jaw and had a scar on his head. Upon examination, the head indeed had a scar, and the mouth was missing two teeth. Simon identified the deceased as his brother. Wei Ligong then conducted a detailed examination, with the three British and French doctors observing. No wounds were found on the head, face, nose, or body, confirming that the death was due to natural causes. The trousers worn by the deceased were also examined and showed signs of diarrhea, further proving that he had suffered from diarrhea before death. Wei Ligong then sawed off a piece of nasal bone and removed the trousers for further detailed analysis.

Interrogation of Brother After Examination: During the examination, Simon Greyteke argued that the deceased's trousers were black and questioned why they were now blue. He wanted to call a witness, Zhibu Dailaifu, to identify them. After the forensic examination, the results were reported to Chief Justice Ying. Judge Wang then instructed the funeral workers to nail the coffin shut and return it to the cold storage. Judge Wang then ordered Simon Greyteke to be interrogated. Simon had already invited witness Zhibu Dailaifu to the scene. The judge asked Simon, "Is this body your brother?" Simon answered, "He has a scar on his head and is missing two teeth, so it is likely him." The judge asked, "The deceased died in the detention center, was examined by the prosecutor, and was collected by Tongren Fu Yuan Funeral Home. Now, Tongren Fu Yuan Funeral Home has opened the coffin. Is that correct?" Simon answered, "Zhibu Dailaifu and my brother were detained together. He knows the color of his trousers. It would be clear if Zhibu Dailaifu could see them." The judge asked, "Did you see them during the examination?" Simon answered, "Yes, I did."

Issue of Trouser Color: The judge asked Zhibu Dailaifu, "The deceased is decomposed. How can you remember clearly?" Zhibu answered, "I can recognize them by looking." The judge ordered a bailiff to take Zhibu Dailaifu to the autopsy room to identify the body. Upon his return, the judge asked, "Is the body Georgie Radikeff? Are the clothes correct?" Zhibu answered, "The clothes were in the prison. He was not wearing them after death." The judge asked Simon, "Do you want to claim the body?" Simon answered, "The color of the trousers is wrong. I am suspicious." The judge then summoned Zhang Yunsheng, an employee of Tongren Fu Yuan Funeral Home, and asked about the collection process. Zhang answered that when they transported the body to the funeral home, the lower body was naked because the trousers were soiled and foul-smelling. Therefore, they were not put on but placed in the coffin. The feet were bare, without shoes. However, the collection record in the funeral home book has the number 1514 marked on the coffin head, so there can be no mistake.

Brother of the Deceased Signs for Coffin: The judge asked Simon again, "Today, we are examining the body of Russian Georgie Radikeff, who died in the detention center on June 19. Do you want to claim it, or should it be buried by Tongren Fu Yuan Funeral Home?" Simon answered, "I cannot say for sure if it is my brother, but I can claim it." The judge said, "You cannot be ambiguous." Simon answered, "I filed a request for examination on the 23rd. Why was it delayed until today? That is illegal." The judge said that the police department filed the lawsuit on July 7, and the trial was held the next day, so there was no delay. The judge added that since it was not his brother, he could not claim it. Simon hesitated for ten minutes and then answered, "I will claim it." The judge then ordered him to sign a receipt for the body. Judge Wang noted on the police department's release form that the body of Georgie Radikeff had been examined and was being claimed by Simon Greyteke for burial. The examination ended at 12:20 PM. During the examination, Zhou Zongxiang, a guard from the defendant detention center, also came to observe before leaving. Simon was taken to the police department by the Western Detective to await further processing.

More Japanese Navy Returning Home Today

Leaving Shanghai on the Tsushima Ship

During the January 28th Incident, almost half of the Japanese navy was dispatched to participate in the fighting. Subsequently, they were gradually withdrawn. The coastal defense ship Tsushima and over 300 sailors remained in Shanghai until the Sasebo reinforcement of 200 marines arrived in Shanghai. Yesterday, the Tsushima and others were ordered to return to Japan.

Naval Withdrawal: The Japanese Naval Ministry dispatched a large naval unit of over 350 officers and sailors to Shanghai after the outbreak of the war. Today, they were ordered to withdraw, and their replacements have already been transported by the Nojima special service ship. The officers and sailors of the unit, along with their firearms and ammunition, boarded the specially dispatched transport ships Sakura Maru and Fengtian Maru, which docked at the Huishan Wharf in Yangshupu at 9:30 AM yesterday. They departed Shanghai, heading directly to the Sasebo Naval Port.

Departure of Tsushima: The Japanese coastal defense ship Tsushima, with a displacement of over 5,000 tons, also participated in the Japanese attack on Wusong. Today, it was ordered to return to Japan. Yesterday at 10:00 AM, it docked at the Huishan Wharf. Representatives of the Shanghai Japanese community, including Miri, Morika, Mitsui President Hayashi, and Naval Attaché to Shanghai Kitaoka, along with Major General Kuwahara and students from the Japanese Resident Elementary School, as well as veterans, came to see them off. Commander Sakonji of the Third Fleet sent a military band to the wharf to play music. At 10:10 AM, the ship departed Shanghai, heading directly back to Japan.

Joint Committee to Convene Meeting Tomorrow

To Discuss the Issue of Japanese Troops in the D District

Regarding the withdrawal of Japanese troops from the D District, Japanese representative Okazaki has broken his promise twice recently. Chinese committee member Yu Hongjun decided yesterday to send a letter to Joint Committee member Cunningham, requesting that the Joint Committee be convened to resolve the issue. After back-and-forth negotiations, it has been decided to hold a meeting tomorrow (the 15th) at 10:00 AM to jointly discuss a solution.

Proposal to Convene a Meeting: Yesterday around 11:00 AM, due to the Japanese side breaking their promise twice, not only violating the spirit of the agreement but also violating international trust, Joint Committee member Yu Hongjun officially submitted a document to Chairman Cunningham requesting that a meeting of the entire committee be convened to jointly discuss and resolve the issue as soon as possible. The letter was sent out yesterday morning. An excerpt is as follows: (Omitted above) The Japanese troops in the D District and at the Hua Feng, Gong Da Feng Tian, and San Sha factories should have been completely withdrawn a month ago in accordance with the agreement signed on May 5. However, after a long period of time, the Japanese side has repeatedly expressed its intention to withdraw, but the result has been consistent delays without any sincere and definite response. Therefore, our committee reported the Japanese side's unreasonable delays to your honorable chairman on the 2nd of this month and requested your strong urging. We are extremely grateful for your repeated urging, but the Japanese side's excuses remain the same. Subsequently, the Japanese side also expressed several times to our committee, but only a small part of the Hua Feng yarn factory in Wusong was withdrawn as a result. After a meeting with Japanese representative Okazaki again on the 6th of this month, Okazaki promised to respond twice but failed to fulfill either promise. This case could have been brought to the Joint Committee for discussion long ago, but we always hoped that the Japanese side would uphold international credibility and withdraw immediately within the shortest possible time. Unfortunately, given the past attitude of the Japanese side, the provisions of the agreement have not been fulfilled. It is regrettable. The reason for having four temporary resident areas in the armistice agreement signed on May 5 was to accommodate the large number of Japanese troops and designate them as temporary resident areas. Now, the Japanese army has been completely withdrawn, and the vicinity of Shanghai has returned to its original state before the January 28th Incident. In accordance with the provisions of Article 3 of the agreement, the Japanese side should immediately withdraw the troops in the D District and at the Gong Da Feng Tian to within the areas beyond the concession boundaries (within the concession) in order to maintain the spirit of the agreement and to have the Japanese side express a definite date for withdrawal. Please, Mr. Chairman, convene a meeting of all committee members immediately to discuss, etc.

Joint Committee to Meet Tomorrow: Yu first handed the letter directly to Secretary Langer to be forwarded and then notified Langer by telephone. Subsequently, he received a reply from Langer stating that the matter had been forwarded to Cunningham and Japanese representative Okazaki had been notified. It was decided to hold the meeting at 10:00 AM on the 15th because the 14th is the French National Day, and it was feared that the French representative would be unable to attend. The location will still be the American Consulate.

Representative of Mongolian Border Cavalry Describes

Anti-Japanese Efforts in Northern Liaoning

Reception for Shanghai Press Yesterday Afternoon

Appeal for Aid to Shanghai

Cheng Changkui, commander of the Mongolian Border Cavalry of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Army, recently sent representatives Zhuang Tianmin, Li Yingkai, and Huang Zhendong, chairman of the Shanghai Youth Volunteer Death Squad Anti-Japanese National Salvation Corps, to Shanghai to request aid from all sectors. Yesterday afternoon, they hosted a reception for the press, where Huang Zhendong reported on the Shanghai Youth Volunteer Death Squad Anti-Japanese National Salvation Corps's joining the Mongolian Border Cavalry and detailed the anti-Japanese combat. Huang said that the Shanghai Youth Volunteer Death Squad Anti-Japanese National Salvation Corps, led by chairman Huang Zhendong, left Shanghai on June 7 and arrived in Ping on June 11. They then traveled through Recha Mongolian to Hei Yuanma, walking to the Ke Lu area. Along the way, they were warmly welcomed by the local authorities, and the commander of the Mongolian Border Cavalry, Cheng Changkui. Upon arriving in Ke Lu, they learned that the Re Border was in critical condition. The Mongolian Border Cavalry, stationed in Tongliao and Ke Lu, Liaoning Province, was bravely resisting the enemy. The team determined that the Tong-Ke area was a crucial area between Liaoning and Re Provinces. If anything untoward happened, Rehe would not be secure. It would be difficult to abandon what was near to save what was far away. Therefore, they immediately joined the force to fight the enemy together, in accordance with the principle that whoever resists Japan, we will support them. Huang also said that the commander of the Mongolian Border Cavalry, Cheng Changkui, is from Liaoyang County, Liaoning Province, and is 42 years old. He graduated from the first class of the Northeast Martial Arts Academy and has held important positions in the military. Last year, he served as the chief of staff of the Mongolian Border Cavalry in northern Liaoning and as the commander of the central route. Now, he has been reorganized as the commander of the Mongolian Border Cavalry Detachment. Since the September 18th Incident, he has led his cavalry unit to occupy Tongliao and the Dalin Dahan area on the Siping-Taonan branch line, advancing towards Liaoyuan. However, due to the loss of Heishan County, which was occupied by friendly forces, and the intense shelling by enemy air force and artillery, they gradually became unsustainable after two days and nights of fierce fighting and retreated to the west of Tongliao. Both sides suffered heavy casualties in this battle. On December 14, after reorganizing his unit, he advanced east to Xishutong and encountered the enemy. After a fierce battle lasting one day and night, the enemy retreated. Our army immediately pursued and recovered Bola Huoshao Temple, Wafang, Liufangdi, Liujia Yuanzi, Sifangdi, Hujia Yuanzi, Wanglao Huiwopu, Yujian Company, and other places. In this battle, our army suffered few casualties, while the enemy suffered over 100 dead and 70 wounded. They also captured many spoils of war. On February 11, our army advanced to Yuliang Fort and encountered the enemy. On the 12th, they were surrounded by the enemy five times. Commander Cheng led his troops to use his self-invented flat-trajectory artillery to inflict heavy casualties. After a fierce battle lasting three days and nights, they finally repelled the enemy. In this battle, they killed a Japanese commander named Yushan and over 50 soldiers, wounded hundreds, and captured one enemy telescope, a full set of military maps, two machine guns, one cannon, and countless weapons and ammunition. Our army suffered over 70 wounded and over 30 dead. On March 17, they fought the enemy at Yingli Temple. After one day and night, the enemy retreated. Our army immediately pursued to Sanhuitang. On March 25, our army advanced to Sanhuitang. The enemy launched a fierce counterattack on our army. Our soldiers, risking their lives, resisted vigorously. After a fierce battle lasting two days and nights, the enemy finally retreated. Both sides suffered heavy casualties in this battle. So far, they have resisted for more than half a year and have fought the enemy dozens of times, finally preserving the corner of Tongliao until now. Of the more than 50 counties in Liaoning Province, this is the only area of a hundred square miles that has not been captured by the enemy. Now, the Re Border is in critical condition, and our army is at the forefront. If anything untoward happens, Rehe will be in danger. Since our army began resisting Japan, tens of thousands of patriotic people from home and abroad have come to join us, causing difficulties in supplies. In the current hot weather, many soldiers are still wearing leather and cotton uniforms, which is extremely miserable. Furthermore, ammunition is scarce, with each soldier averaging less than ten bullets. Therefore, while confronting the enemy across the river, they have sent representatives to Shanghai to appeal to patriotic people from all walks of life, requesting immediate and full support to recover the lost territory in the Northeast. The representatives will return to the battlefield to kill the enemy immediately after negotiations are completed.

French Water and Electricity Company Employees to Resume Work Today

General Meeting Resolves to Accept Municipal Government Order

All Terms Awaiting Resolution by Authorities

After the strike by all employees of the mechanical department of the French Water and Electricity Company, the strong attitude of the company made it impossible for party and government agencies to mediate. Yesterday, a general meeting resolved to accept the order of the Municipal Government and resume work today, with all terms awaiting resolution by the authorities.

Water and Electricity Company Statement: The French Water and Electricity Company issued a statement saying that according to reports in various newspapers regarding the strike of the French tram and electricity workers, it seems that various parties are actively engaged in negotiations to mediate. It is hereby declared that this information is absolutely inaccurate. According to Chinese law, this strike is completely illegal, and any mediation is out of the question. The company also knows that both the Chinese and French authorities are fully aware of this.

Direct Labor-Management Consultation: The strike committee of the Second Special District Water and Electricity Industry Union sent representatives Shen Jingyi, Zhang Fubao, Chen Adi, Yu Guixiang, and others to the company at 2:00 PM yesterday. Accompanied by the comprador Yu Jingshan as translator, they met with the superintendent Kuchya and presented their demands, hoping that they would be accepted. The superintendent replied that the company welcomes the workers to return to work and guarantees their safety. The representatives then left at 2:30 PM.

Municipal Government Orders Resumption of Work: The Municipal Government accepted the request of French Consul General Méléariat and immediately ordered the French Water and Electricity workers to resume work and await a resolution. Xu Yefu, the third section chief of the Social Affairs Bureau, also summoned the union leaders Shen Jingyi and Zhang Fubao to persuade them to consider international relations and local security and resume work immediately, with all terms awaiting resolution by the authorities.

Union Issues Notice: The strike committee of the Second Special District Water and Electricity Industry Union issued a notice to all members yesterday, stating that a general meeting will be held at the Xiaoximen Youth Lecture Group at 2:00 PM on July 13. All members are required to attend on time. It is hereby notified. By 1:00 PM, all employees gathered on Luban Road and marched in formation to the Youth Lecture Group for the meeting. Zhou Lianze from the Municipal Party Committee and Zhu Lin from the Social Affairs Bureau attended to provide guidance. Later, the Second Division of the Second District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, not having received orders from the headquarters, prohibited the assembly. The representatives of the party and government agencies explained the reasons to the headquarters, and the misunderstanding was resolved. However, all employees had already marched back to the union headquarters to await orders.

General Meeting of All Members: The Municipal Public Security Bureau, having approved the general meeting by the party and government agencies, sent the eighth squadron of the police brigade and police officers from the Second District Police Station, all armed, led by District Chief Zhang Kaitong, to Luban Road to provide protection. The meeting was then announced. The surrounding area was maintained by the picket team and police officers, with strict precautions. Shen Jingyi, Zhang Fubao, Cai Amei, and others were elected as the presidium, and Shen Naiwen recorded the minutes. First, the chairman reported on the negotiations by the party and government agencies and the Municipal Government's order to persuade them to resume work, with all terms to be negotiated with the French consul by the authorities, ensuring a final victory. Subsequently, Zhou Lianze from the Municipal Party Committee and Zhu Guilin from the Social Affairs Bureau repeatedly urged the workers to trust the government and consider international relations. Therefore, a resolution was passed on the spot that all would accept the order of the Municipal Government and resume work from the 14th, with all terms to be handled by the party and government agencies. The meeting adjourned at 7:00 PM. At the same time, the police brigade withdrew.

French National Day Today

Lantern Parade Cancelled Last Night

Military Parade Held This Morning

Today is French National Day. In the past, the French Concession in Shanghai has always had grand celebrations on this day. All institutions and fire stations in the concession competed to decorate with lanterns, and a lantern parade was held on the eve of the holiday along Rue du Consulat and Avenue Joffre, full of dazzling colors. The French authorities originally intended to expand the celebrations as much as possible this time. However, due to the recent labor unrest in Shanghai, there was deep concern that lawless elements might take the opportunity to cause trouble. Therefore, they temporarily changed their initial plans, and the lantern parade last night was cancelled. However, the military parade in the French Park this morning was still held as usual. However, the park entrance tickets that were traditionally distributed by the French Municipal Council were also cancelled at the same time.

Jiangnan

New Risks Frequently Arising in Dike Work

Urgent Need to Repair 1,500 Zhang of Engineering

Estimated Cost of Labor and Materials Approximately 600,000 Yuan

Rehabilitation Committee Urgently Cables Government Requesting Appropriation

The members of the Jiangnan Dike Rehabilitation Committee, including Mu Ouchu, believe that the dike works are facing financial difficulties and the consequences are unimaginable. Yesterday, they sent a letter to Chairman Gu and a telegram to Premier Wang of the government, requesting a swift appropriation of funds. The original texts are transcribed below:

Letter to the Chairman: A letter from Mu Ouchu, a member of the committee, to the chairman of the committee, states: "Chairman Mo San, greetings. We met in Shanghai, and it has been a month since then. I hope you are well and prosperous, and I pray for you. Since the establishment of the Dike Works Association, nearly three months have passed. Fortunately, with your able leadership and the diligence of all colleagues, the project is progressing relatively quickly. If there are no special changes, the projects that have already started should be completed before the big flood. However, after the war in Shanghai, the people are impoverished and resources are exhausted. We previously received a transfer of 700,000 yuan in grain transport bonds, which, after repeated negotiations with banks, only yielded 310,000 yuan in silver dollars. Recently, fortunately, the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau and the Money Guild have guaranteed 70,000 yuan, leaving a shortage of 20,000 yuan from the originally planned 400,000 yuan. We will try our best to raise enough funds to fulfill our mission. However, the labor and material costs for the projects that have already started, along with various necessary administrative and reserve expenses, cannot be managed without 550,000 yuan. After deducting the 400,000 yuan borrowed, there is still a shortage of 150,000 yuan. The city also has a similar shortage. Although we have repeatedly appealed to the central government, we have not received a single cent of assistance. As for the social aspect, borrowing 400,000 yuan has already required repeated persuasion, and it is still insufficient. It is really impossible to start raising donations from scratch. Considering the government's high expectations and the urgent need for our hometown, I am anxious and unsure what to do. According to reports from the heads of various engineering departments, there are still about 1,500 zhang of engineering that have not yet started but urgently need to be repaired (a detailed list is attached separately). The estimated cost of labor and materials is really 600,000 yuan. After I, along with Committee Member Zhang Xiaoliang and Committee Member Shen Lisun, went to inspect, all the reports were accurate. If we ignore it, repairing here will lead to collapse there, and the state's huge funds will be wasted, and the local hidden worries will remain. If we continue the repair, there will be no funding. I am compelled to join the other members of the committee in sending a telegram to Premier Wang, describing the actual situation and requesting a large appropriation of funds (the telegram has already been published in this newspaper on the 10th and is omitted here). However, the central government's recent financial situation has long been known to us. If empty words are of no help, how can we manage the rehabilitation? I always advocate pragmatism in handling affairs. Since I have witnessed the dangerous situation and am deeply aware of the local economic difficulties and the inability to raise donations, I dare not fail to report the actual situation to you in detail, awaiting your wise guidance. Furthermore, although part of this year's project has been repaired, there are still many places that have not been repaired. The river water has already risen, and the autumn flood will inevitably be severe. Disaster relief equipment must be prepared in advance. The committee's responsibility is rehabilitation, and it has no authority to advise on this annual repair and disaster relief project. I and my colleagues are engaged in commerce and cannot devote ourselves fully to the committee's affairs. I also request that you order the responsible department to make proper preparations to avoid being rushed when the time comes and making mistakes in both areas. I cannot express my respect enough in this letter. I respectfully wish you good health. Mu Xiangyue."

Urgent Engineering Projects: List of Jiangnan Dike projects urgently needing continued work: Provincial Area, Baoshan Section: Chenhua Bank, 115 zhang; Gu Long Pier, 456 zhang; Zhangjia House, 105 zhang; Stone Cave, 133 zhang; Provincial Area, Changtai Section: Chu Chengjing, 77 zhang; Yueyue Terrace, 60 zhang; Yanglin, 60 zhang; Yongzi Field, 50 zhang; Qianjing, 60 zhang; Provincial Area, Songjiang Section: Section 1, 60 zhang; Section 2, 136 zhang; Section 5, 90 zhang; Section 6, 100 zhang. Total: 1,502 zhang.

New County Government Office Begins Construction

Completion Expected by Year-End, Construction Cost Over 70,000 Yuan

The Shanghai County Government, last year, designated fifty mu of land near the North Bridge Town on North Huiji Road for the construction of a new county government office. Since the January 28th Incident, the construction plan has been suspended indefinitely. Now that order in Shanghai has been restored, the construction of the new office has begun on the previous day. The budget is over 70,000 yuan for construction costs, and it is expected to be completed by the end of this year. The new office will be open on New Year's Day next year. The style of the new office will be modeled after the new city government, and a zoo will be built in front of the county government office.

Zhang Ming Talks About

The Patriotic People of Nepal

Last year, in order to strengthen diplomatic relations between China and Nepal, the government specially sent Zhang Dingcheng to Nepal as a representative of the government to award the Grand Marshal of Nepal the rank of General of the Army of the Republic of China and the First Class Baoding Medal. After his mission, he received a grand welcome from the government and people of Nepal. In February of this year, the King of Nepal presented Ambassador Zhang with the Second Class Glorious Precious Star of Nepal. This time, he was summoned back to the country by telegram from Chairman Chiang. Because he passed through tropical areas such as India and Burma, he contracted an illness en route and made a brief stop in Shanghai, so he could not proceed immediately. It is said that Ambassador Zhang once served as Consul-General in India, Java, and other places and is well aware of the national conditions of those countries. This time, he was ordered to go to Nepal, and the people of Nepal deeply appreciated our country's generosity and wished to establish eternal friendship. The reporter found it strange that Nepal was originally a tributary state of our country, and its area is only 500 li and its width is no more than 1,500 li. How can it stand between China and India? According to Ambassador Zhang's findings, he made the following remarks: (1) The people of Nepal are courteous, righteous, and have simple customs and can adhere to the old Eastern morality. (2) The people are hard-working and good at fighting. The country's military preparedness is well-maintained, with a regular army of 100,000 and a reserve army of 200,000. Military equipment and ammunition are sufficient for self-defense. If there is a foreign invasion, the people will rise up to resist the enemy without the need for government mobilization, and the government also values public opinion. With unity from top to bottom, strong neighbors dare not covet it. (3) The people of Nepal hate using foreign goods. All household utensils are domestically produced. Moreover, the country is small and the population is sparse, so it is not subject to the restrictions of tariffs and the constraints of consular jurisdiction. It is completely a free country, which is very different from our country, which has a large land and a large population, but is not as strong as a small country. This really fills me with endless feelings.

The Sino-Foreign Famine Relief Committee Takes Responsibility

Gaoyou Dike Project to Be Completed Soon

The Achievements of Layman Lin Yin Destroying His Family

The Completion Ceremony Will Be Held on a Selected Date

During the severe autumn floods last year, the left bank of the Grand Canal, from the Six Gates of Jiangdu to the Dangjun Bridge of Gaoyou, had 27 breaches. Lakes and rivers merged into one, stretching for more than sixty li. The losses of life and property suffered by the nine counties north of the Yangtze River cannot be enumerated. The Shanghai Sino-Foreign Famine Relief Committee appealed for donations at home and abroad and engaged in emergency relief, with remarkable results. At that time, the great philanthropist Layman Lin Yin heard of this with compassion, destroyed his family to relieve the disaster, and donated 200,000 yuan to the committee. His heart of relieving the hunger and drowning of others can truly be called the embroidered Buddha of ten thousand families. Later, when the water level of the Grand Canal receded slightly, the Canal Works Rehabilitation Committee sent personnel to block the breaches and cut off the flow at various breaches. The Sino-Foreign Famine Relief Committee believed that dike repair work could both provide work as relief and fundamentally eliminate future floods, so it resolutely negotiated with the authorities and took responsibility for the dike construction project at the six major breaches in Gaoyou. The budget for the project was over 400,000 yuan. In addition to the 200,000 yuan donated by Layman Lin Yin, there was still a significant shortfall. However, the committee did not worry about it. In addition to actively soliciting donations, it also hired Canal Works Committee member Wang Shuxiang to preside over the engineering work and started work immediately. As of June of this year, four of the six breach projects have been completed in order. The remaining two locations, Dangjun Tower and Miaohangkou, are also imminent. The so-called six breaches are: Dangjun Tower, Miaoxiangkou, Yumatou, Qigongdian, Ershilipu, and Sanshilipu. A summary of the project is recorded below:

Breach Situation: (1) Dangjun Tower has always been a dangerous project, with a breach length of 160 zhang and a depth of about 3 zhang. (2) Miaohangkou has a breach length of 64 zhang and a depth of 1 zhang and 2.5 chi. (3) Yumatou has a breach length of 15 zhang and a depth of 1 zhang and 2.4 chi. (4) Qigongdian has a breach length of 22.5 zhang and a depth of 1 zhang and 1.9 chi. The above four locations are all in the northwest of the city. There are also Ershilipu and Sanshilipu, both in the south of the city. The breach length of Liushilipu is 62 zhang and the depth is over 1 zhang. The breach length of Sanshilipu is 67.5 zhang and the depth is 1 zhang and 2.7 chi. This is a general overview of the measurement of the six breaches.

Project Overview: Except for Ershilipu, the breaches were all brick and stone projects in the past. Last year's breaches caused almost all the bricks and stones to be washed away by the water. The dike restoration project was originally intended to still use bricks and stones or temporarily replace them with concrete. Later, due to the lack of time, it was changed to adding brushwood and straw to the earthwork to increase resistance during this year's autumn floods. Brushwood is soft and elastic. Even if it is impacted by huge waves, it will not be damaged. Using softness to control softness is no less effective than bricks and stones. However, after the start of this construction, it has been particularly difficult to obtain soil. The Dangjun Tower project needs to transport 44,000 square meters of soil. There are dam dikes built on both ends of the canal, and soil boats cannot reach it directly. The nearby fields are flooded and the soil is not suitable for construction, so all the soil required for this project is transported from four or five li away. It takes a lot of effort to build bridges and embankments. There are thousands of soil boats gathered at Dangjun Tower, with three people per boat. Every fifty boats are organized into a team. They recognize their flags and advance and retreat in an orderly manner. There are an average of three to four thousand laborers per day engaged in bailing water, carrying soil, and driving piles, all of whom are local disaster victims. There are also nearly two hundred staff members taking care of the dike work. This only applies to Dangjun Tower. Although the other five locations do not use as much soil or have as many staff members, the difficulties in hiring laborers and obtaining soil are the same as at Dangjun Tower. The modification methods for the six breaches are listed below: (Dangjun Tower) The length of the project is 167 zhang. The width of the top of the straw and soil is 4 zhang. The height is 2 zhang and 2.9 chi. The new slope has three contractions. The height of the straw is 2 zhang and 0.8 chi. The face soil is 8 cun thick, level with the top of the soil. The straw does not fill the pond. The inside and outside have three contractions. (Miaohangkou) The length of the project is 64 zhang. The width of the top of the straw and soil is 4 zhang. The height of the sac is 2 zhang and 1.5 chi. The new slope has three contractions. The height of the straw is 1 zhang and 7.6 chi. The face soil is 8 cun thick, level with the top of the soil. The straw is filled to a height of 4 chi at the bottom, with two contractions on one side. (Yumatou) The length of the project is 15 zhang. The width of the new top is 3 zhang. The length of the fur is 1 zhang and 6.2 chi. The new slope has three contractions. The outside height is 1 zhang and 7.5 chi. The new slope has two contractions. (Qigongdian) The length of the project is 22.5 zhang. The width of the top of the straw and soil is 4 zhang. The inside height is 1 zhang and 6 cun. The new slope has three contractions. The height of the straw is 1 zhang and 6.7 chi. The face soil is 8 cun thick, level with the top of the soil. (Ershilipu) The length of the project is 62 zhang. The width of the new top is 3 zhang. The inside height is 2 zhang and 2.4 chi. The new slope has three contractions. The outside height is 1 zhang and 8.1 chi. The new slope has two contractions, level with both ends. (Sanshilipu) The length of the project is 67.5 zhang. The total width of the straw work is 4 zhang. The inside height is 2 zhang and 5.2 chi. The new slope has three contractions. The inside height is 1 zhang and 6 chi. The face soil is 8 cun thick, level with the top of the soil. Currently, four of the above six dike projects have been completed according to the above measurements (Sanshilipu, Liushilipu, Qigongdian, Yumatou). The Sino-Foreign Famine Relief Committee is also responsible for the 853.7 zhang of flat work near the six breaches, including helping to raise, reinforce, and fill the gaps. This project has also been completed. Although this type of dike construction uses soil as a raw material, purely using soil to build up the dikes, with such great height and depth, and such a wide length, new soil and new work are difficult to consolidate. Therefore, pilings have been added to places such as Dangjun Tower, Miaoxiangkou, Sanshilipu, and Qigongdian. The names of the pilings are Guant, Guansao, and Qiansao. Approximately 4,000 pilings have been used in the four breaches, with lengths ranging from 2 zhang and 4 chi to over 3 zhang. Like the human body, soil is the muscle, and wooden piles are the skeleton.

Money Is Not Wasted: The original budget for the six breach projects was over 400,000 yuan, but based on current calculations, less than 400,000 yuan will be enough. This is due to the cheap price of soil and the integrity of the engineering staff. According to the desire for good engineering, personal supervision is necessary. Therefore, the six breach projects were presided over by Wang Shuxiang, who personally supervised the work day and night, so that the goal of not wasting money and returning the work to reality could be achieved. The Sino-Foreign Famine Relief Committee is naturally employing the right person, and Layman Lin Yin, who destroyed his family to relieve the disaster, must also be happy and deeply grateful that the six breaches will soon be fully completed, returning our entire dike and protecting northern Jiangsu. It is heard that the committee plans to send personnel to hold a completion ceremony at that time and invite the Jiangsu Provincial Government to inspect and accept the project.

Department Telegram

Resolving the Wenzhou-Chuzhou Salt Affairs Dispute

The people of Wenzhou and Chuzhou oppose the contractor system. Those in Shanghai have organized an improvement association, and Yongshou and other Frenchmen have also jointly organized an improvement association, actively petitioning. The Transportation Envoy has forwarded it to the office. The Transport Office received a telegram from the Department the other day, which is transcribed as follows: Zhou Transport Envoy, please read. Salt New Secret. The Transportation Envoy's No. 210 submission and attachments have been received. The contractor Wang Yongshan in Wenzhou and Chuzhou has been repeatedly accused. According to the Transportation Envoy's investigation and submission, the contractor has not handled the matter perfectly and cannot satisfy the local people. For the sake of fundamental rectification, the only option is to take it back and run it officially, and still follow the previous open method, so that anyone can pay taxes and transport salt. This should be approved. However, during the transition of taking it back and running it officially, there are urgent matters to be prepared. For example, whether Wang Yongshan has owed any taxes since he took office, and whether there are any unfulfilled permits and unsold salt, the Transportation Envoy should quickly investigate and clarify. If there are any unpaid taxes, they should be immediately recovered. Unfulfilled permits and unsold salt should be investigated and dealt with in accordance with Article 7 of the Wenzhou-Chuzhou Recognized Merchant Regulations. As for the various fees collected by Wang Yongshan in the salt price during his tenure, the Transportation Envoy should follow the instructions of the Salt Affairs Bureau of this Department, Renzi No. 831, and investigate thoroughly and demand payment within a time limit. The merchant patrol equipment and clothing purchased by Wang Yongshan were paid for by the recognized merchant from the patrol subsidy collected from the salt price, which was originally borne by the people and not purchased by the merchant himself. They should be ordered to hand over all of them to the public for inventory, without giving any compensation. Furthermore, according to the Transportation Envoy's previous telegrams, the salt reserves in Wenzhou and Chuzhou were exhausted early, and no Min salt was imported. Please allow the borrowing of 100,000 Jin of Huai salt to alleviate the salt shortage. After the cancellation of the Wenzhou-Chuzhou contractor, whether the salt reserves produced in various salt fields in Wenzhou and Chuzhou can meet the needs of free sales after opening, and if they are insufficient, how should they be supplied? If it is necessary to borrow from other areas, how should it be handled to ensure accurate transportation and sales? The Transportation Envoy should investigate and clarify these matters together and propose a solution quickly. If there are other matters that need to be prepared, the Transportation Envoy should carefully plan and submit them for review and handling. In short, the Wenzhou-Chuzhou contractor has not been managed well and should be revoked, but national taxes and people's food must be taken into account. We must speed up preparations and carry out the work earnestly, so as to achieve rectification as soon as possible. Please comply and report the handling situation to be checked as needed. Ministry of Finance, slight seal.

The Problem of Abolishing the Tael and Changing to the Yuan

Yesterday, this newspaper published a certain gentleman's remarks on abolishing the tael and changing to the yuan, discussing customs duties, foreign exchange, domestic remittances, debts, claims, national currency, and banknotes. The words were concise and insightful, providing excellent material for researchers. However, abolishing the tael and changing to the yuan is a major event. Many people in the country advocate making a decisive decision and proceeding quickly, but there are also those who advocate careful consideration and advance planning for various methods of dealing with the aftermath. This newspaper will further disclose the opinions of those who advocate caution, as follows:

The gentleman whose opinions are published today is a financial giant in Shanghai, who has been engaged in business in Shanghai for decades. He has also served in the current firm for more than ten years. He is knowledgeable about financial affairs and often makes accurate predictions. His words may be used as a source of inspiration for others. The gentleman said:

Regarding the matter of abolishing the tael and changing to the yuan, those who advocate a positive approach are indeed urging its success, and those who advocate a negative approach need not oppose it. Consider this a matter of fact, but the key is to ensure that there are sufficient funds after the change to the yuan, so as not to directly shake the finances and indirectly disrupt commerce. As for what we think should be paid attention to, let us try to speak about it, knowing that we will be blamed, but not caring.

Shanghai is currently a market that uses silver (the reporter notes that this is the so-called silver terminal), not only for money shops, which mostly use silver as the standard, but also for all domestic remittances, which are mostly converted in silver taels. Moreover, foreign trade mainly uses silver taels, and foreign banks are even engaged in collecting and storing silver as reserves. Therefore, although silver dollars are used in market transactions, silver taels are used in commerce, remittances, and foreign trade. Furthermore, Shanghai is a terminal where cash is received and delivered daily. When receiving and delivering, silver taels are always used. Therefore, the power of silver taels in the market can be imagined. Now that the tael is abolished and changed to the yuan, the financial industry has important relationships with customers and in mutual settlements, which should be paid attention to. However, domestic and foreign remittances can be calculated at the legal price, which may not be a problem.

As for customers, in the current financial industry, there are many foreign accounts and also many silver accounts. As Shanghai has always been a silver terminal, depositors who deposit silver taels must also be paid in silver taels when they withdraw. Now that the tael is abolished and changed to the yuan, silver dollars will naturally be given according to regulations. Furthermore, mutual settlements originally used silver, but now that the yuan has been changed, silver dollars should also be used for mutual settlements.

Originally, Shanghai was a silver terminal, and the national currency, silver dollars, has always been insufficient (the reporter notes that the current Shanghai market claims to have 200 million silver dollars, but in fact it may be no more than 150 to 160 million taels). The hard currency that is currently circulating actually contains less than seven qian of pure silver, but it is used as a representative of a market price of over seven qian (the price fluctuates and is called yangli). Moreover, due to the inevitable phenomenon of bad money driving out good money, provinces such as Guangdong, Jiangsu, Hubei, and other provinces, as well as Yuan dollars, are now being melted down into silver, amounting to tens of thousands of yuan per day (the reporter notes that melting down Guangdong dollars and Yuan dollars into silver, calculated at the current yangli, can yield nearly 200 taels of profit per 10,000 yuan). As a result, the hard currency circulating in the market is actually below its legal representative price. If the tael is abolished and changed to the yuan and these silver dollars are used as the exchange product for abolishing the tael, will silver depositors not suffer losses? This is the first thing that needs special attention.

It is well known that there is currently an insufficient supply of hard currency. After the abolishment of the tael, in order to alleviate the shortage of hard currency, banknotes will inevitably be used. However, China has been issuing banknotes for decades, such as the official money notes of Hubei and the Feng banknotes of the three northeastern provinces. Occasionally, due to incidents, they have either been cancelled in form or fallen to unimaginable levels. People who hold banknotes have suffered incalculable losses. Now, feeling the insufficient supply of hard currency and using banknotes, it will inevitably increase the amount of banknotes issued. In normal times, the circulation of banknotes is fine, but if there is a slight incident and a storm arises, the credibility of banknotes will inevitably become a problem again. In the past, with silver taels and silver dollars coexisting, and silver taels being the mainstay of market circulation, and with silver stored in reserves, it was still enough to use silver taels to settle the shortage of silver dollars. Now that the yuan has been changed, if the yuan is insufficient, even if banknotes are used, the credibility of banknotes will be a problem, and the market turmoil will be even greater.

For the current plan, the first thing to pay attention to when abolishing the tael and changing to the yuan is silver dollars. In short, it should be divided into two points:

(1) The fineness of silver dollars. The amount of pure silver contained in silver dollars should be equal to the value it represents and should not be reduced in the slightest. As for the legal price regulations, the government has the right to weigh them and formulate them based on the content. For example, if the amount of pure silver contained in each silver dollar is six qian and eight fen, then when the tael is abolished, the legal price of each yuan should not be higher than six qian and eight fen. If the legal price matches the pure silver, then when the tael is abolished and changed to the yuan, silver depositors will not lose money.

(2) Adding the minting of hard currency. There is currently an insufficient supply of hard currency for circulation, which is inconvenient once the tael is abolished. Therefore, the government should immediately add the minting of hard currency to ensure a steady supply that is sufficient for circulation in the national market, without having to wait for banknotes. If hard currency is sufficient and the fineness is uniform, then there will be enough cash for exchange, and silver taels can be cancelled without any problems.

Furthermore, minting hard currency cannot be done quickly enough, so banknotes must be used temporarily. There should also be stricter regulations for banknotes:

(1) Issuing a fixed amount. Banks that issue banknotes today have a fixed amount, and the total amount issued rises and falls with the amount of circulation. Once the tael is abolished, the demand for banknotes will increase greatly, and those with the right to issue banknotes will inevitably increase the issuance due to the increase in demand. However, if the increase is too much and the amount is not fixed, even if the credit is good, how can everyone know about it? It is best for each bank to measure its own ability and set a total issuance amount. No matter what, the issuance should not exceed this amount. Then society will know that the bank's strength is sufficient to bear the burden, and its issuance credit will increase and its circulation will be smoother.

(2) Strict inspection. Today, those who issue banknotes have mostly implemented an inspection system. In the future, after the tael is abolished, the circulation of banknotes will be of great importance to the whole country. An extremely open and strict inspection should be carried out, and those responsible for the inspection should especially know that the people's livelihood and the country's destiny depend on it. They must not be afraid of hard work or show favoritism. All reserves of cash and securities should be personally checked one by one to show great credibility. Then the credit of banknotes will increase and the power of circulation will expand.

In short, to abolish the tael and change to the yuan, there must first be sufficient preparation and advance planning so that after the system is changed, the people will not have the slightest inconvenience or loss and there will be no further disputes. This is what the people hope for and what the financial industry should be responsible for. We hope to encourage each other with the people of the country to achieve success and offer our blessings.

Local News Two

Guo Luman

Marriage Dispute Case

Divided into Three Major Parts

To be Tried by Three Judges

Identity Case Suspended

Awaiting Public Prosecution Verdict for Further Hearing

Guo Luman, a native of Ningbo who owns a substantial amount of real estate and is past his prime, has a wife, Han Yueling, who has borne him three daughters. The eldest has already married out, and the youngest is also fifteen years old. Unexpectedly, Guo, on May 29th of this year, falsely claimed to have divorced Han and formally married Xu Zhiqing, a female painter from the City Temple, thus committing the crime of bigamy. Han not only requested the police to initiate a public prosecution against Guo but also retained lawyers Yang Linzhi and Zhang Jiahui to file a private prosecution against Xu Zhiqing for knowingly marrying a married man. Xu's uncle, Xu Guanchen, and the matchmakers Lian Jiming and Xing Chunhua, were also accused of aiding bigamy. Guo Luman, on the other hand, filed a civil suit against Han Yueling, claiming that Han's status as his wife had been extinguished by the divorce papers he had drawn up, and requested confirmation of his identity. Xu Zhiqing then also retained lawyer Chen Tingrui to sue Guo for fraudulent marriage, involving Han's younger sisters Qian Hu Miaosheng and Han Meisheng. All of these cases are interconnected. The First Special District Local Court scheduled hearings yesterday, morning and afternoon, to try them separately.

Identity Confirmation Case: At 10:30 AM, Judge Qiao Wanxuan of the Seventh Tribunal first opened the hearing for Guo's case against Han for confirmation of identity. The original plaintiffs and defendants, along with their respective lawyers, reported on time. In addition, many female relatives of both parties were in court to observe. According to the plaintiff, Guo Luman, his marriage to Han was arranged by his parents, but between the tenth and eleventh years of the Republic (1921-1922), he had already drawn up a divorce agreement and published a statement in the newspaper. The divorce papers and newspapers were kept in an iron box, which was taken away by Han. If that evidence is needed, Han should be ordered to hand over the box, etc. Guo's lawyer, Wu Chengyu, then presented a draft letter, stating that this letter was to Guo's father, Yonglan, inquiring whether his son had divorce papers. Although no written reply was received, someone was sent to inquire, and it was claimed that it was indeed the case, but unfortunately, Guo's father was unwilling to testify. Then, the judge questioned Guo and Han, who stated that she had never been divorced by Guo, and there were no so-called divorce papers. Han's lawyer, Yang Linzhi, then cited the Civil Procedure Law, requesting that the case be suspended, stating that because another criminal case was in progress, this case should be temporarily suspended until the criminal proceedings were concluded. This is a procedural issue of great importance, and a ruling is requested first. Guo's lawyer, on the other hand, opposed, saying that the criminal suit should be suspended first, and the criminal suit should be heard after the verdict in this identity suit. After consideration by Judge Qiao, he ruled in court that the civil suit should be suspended pending the conclusion of the criminal proceedings. He adjourned the court, and the clock struck eleven.

Police Prosecution Case: After fifteen minutes, the police's public prosecution of Guo Luman for bigamy and Guo and Han's private prosecution of Xu Zhiqing, Xu Guanchen, Lian Jiming, Xing Chunhua, and others for complicity in the marriage were heard by Judge Feng Shide in the First Criminal Tribunal. Thereupon, everyone involved in the case, including lawyers and relatives of both parties, moved from the Seventh Tribunal to the First Tribunal. This court was larger, and the audience was even larger, but most were women. However, the defendant Xu Guanchen and the two matchmakers did not appear in court. According to Xu Zhiqing, her uncle, Guanchen, was ill with anger because he was accused, so it was difficult for him to appear in court. As for the two matchmakers, they were not present because they had left Shanghai. The prosecuting lawyer for the police, Ru Baoyi, first stated that the defendant in the public prosecution was only Guo Luman. The remaining defendants were all privately prosecuted by Guo and Han. These two cases were interconnected. Whether they should be tried together should be considered. Judge Feng then announced that for the convenience of the trial, it was appropriate to try them together, but the public prosecution should not be confused with the private prosecution, so separate verdicts would still be given in the future. The lawyers for each side had no objection to this approach, and the interrogation began immediately. First, Guo Luman was asked if he had found any evidence. Guo's testimony was the same as in the civil court, still claiming that the evidence was hidden in the iron box, and requesting that the case be postponed again to continue searching for evidence. Guo's lawyer also presented the letter to Guo Yonglan, requesting that he be summoned to testify, but all were strongly refuted by the police lawyer, who stated that Guo had said that he had divorced Han, but had not produced any evidence, which was obviously empty talk. Moreover, Guo Yonglan had already published a statement in the newspaper that he was not responsible for his son's bigamy, which showed that there were no divorce papers. In short, the defendant's bigamy was undoubtedly the case. The civil court had suspended the identity suit, awaiting the conclusion of this case before reopening the hearing, so if the defendant's request for postponement was granted, it would not be approved. Judge Feng then questioned Guo and Han, who stated that there were no divorce papers in the iron box. The box had two keys, one for me and one for the defendant. Before the lawsuit, the defendant would often open the box, but after the lawsuit, he had never opened it. She also recounted the details of her private prosecution against Xu Zhiqing and others. The defendant Xu Zhiqing stated that she was twenty-seven years old. On December 24th of the fourteenth year of the Republic (1925), she was engaged to Guo Luman through Lian Jiming and Zhou, the mother of Xing Chunhua. At that time, Guo was living in the Jian De Hui dormitory, and the matchmaker said that Guo's wife was dead and that he was remarried. The following year, when she learned that Guo had a wife, she wanted to dissolve the engagement, but the matchmaker said that Guo had divorced Han. I didn't believe it in the end. Later, Jin Defu showed me Guo's handwritten letter, which said that he had broken off relations with Han. However, after this twist and turn, both parties put this matter aside for seven years. People and in March of this year Zhou of Xing suddenly the younger brother of Hu, Han Meisheng and Hu Miaosheng together to my house, and spoke of the wedding again.

Hu also stated that Guo had already divorced Han, and the family property had also been divided equally between Guo and Han. Guo was determined to marry her. If I still didn't believe it, I could ask a lawyer to testify or have both parents publish a statement in the newspaper. So on May 29th, we got married at the Yangbu Public Office. How could I know that it was all a deception they designed? Her lawyer, Chen Tingrui, presented the wedding advertisement as evidence. Questioning Guo Luman, he said that this was actually a trap set by Han to induce me to do it myself. I have not lived with her for ten years. She was resentful and designed to frame me. When I got engaged to Xu, although I said that I had broken off relations with Han, the woman did not believe me, so the matter was put aside for several years. I had no hope of marrying Xu. Last spring, Han asked me about this, saying why haven't you married her yet? I said I had no money. She immediately ordered her younger brother, Meisheng, to borrow 4,000 yuan from her brother-in-law, Hu Miaosheng, to pay the woman's family as betrothal gifts. At the same time, she accompanied me to rent a house in Gaoshou Lane to use as our new home. Han was also present on the day of the wedding. I heard that her initial plan was to wait for the betrothal gifts to arrive at the door and buy a large number of hooligans to cause trouble so that the police could intervene, and then take the opportunity to accuse me of bigamy. Fortunately, this plan was seen through by my eldest son-in-law, who called Han away beforehand, so fortunately, nothing happened that day, etc. However, Han denied this testimony. Judge Feng inquired until noon and then adjourned the hearing to continue on the morning of the 22nd. Guo Luman was still released on bail of 5,000 yuan.

Private Prosecution for Fraudulent Marriage: At 2:30 PM, Judge Wu Tingqi took the bench in the Second Criminal Tribunal to hear Xu Zhiqing's private prosecution against Guo Luman and others for fraudulent marriage. The plaintiff, Xu Zhiqing, first recounted the details of Han Meisheng and Hu Miaosheng's coming to discuss the marriage, which was roughly the same as what she said in the morning. Her lawyer, Chen Tingrui, further added that this case was actually created by Han. Han Meisheng and others are her younger brothers. The plaintiff believed them, thinking that Han had indeed broken off relations with Guo, and then decided to marry him. Guo Luman then stated that Han and Hu's visit to discuss the marriage was actually done by Han, and at that time, I was still in Hangzhou, etc. Questioning Han, she denied the statements of Xu and Guo. Han Meisheng and Hu Miaosheng both claimed that they did not go to Xu's house to discuss the marriage. Then, lawyer Chen presented the thin receipt for sending the letter and the matchmaker's wedding invitation, proving that Han and Hu had indeed known about it. Guo Luman also stated that the letter presented by lawyer Chen was indeed written by Hu. Hu also had the name Xian Zhang, so the note was signed with the name Xian Zhang, etc. Zheng Ruosun, the second landlord of the house rented by Guo in Gaoshou Lane, proved that Guo and Han came to rent the house together. Judge Wu then adjourned the case to be scheduled after the verdict in the divisible portion.

Murder for Property Case in Pudong

Two Perpetrators Sentenced to Death

Zhang (surname Zhang) Sentenced to Two Years Imprisonment

Zhang Linsen, a deceased racehorse leader in Huayuanshi Bridge, Pudong, had three wives and concubines. After Zhang and his first wife, Zhang Qian, passed away, they left behind property. Disputes arose over the uneven distribution between the legitimate and illegitimate sides. Zhang Qingxiang, the son of Zhang (surname Zhang), the third concubine, colluded with his maternal uncle, Zhang Quansheng, nicknamed "Beef Quansheng," to murder Linsen's eldest son, Guoxiang, and second son, Yuxiang. However, Yuxiang was shot and killed, while Guoxiang was injured but not killed. This case was thoroughly investigated by the prosecutor of the Local Court, who prosecuted Zhang Qingxiang and Zhang Quansheng for premeditated murder, and Zhang (surname Zhang) for joint murder. Judge Shen Youqi of the Criminal Tribunal repeatedly opened hearings to investigate and extensively consulted public opinion. After tireless research, he announced the end of the debate a few days ago. Zhang Guoxiang and Zhang Bao, the wife of Zhang Yuxiang, both filed private suits for compensation for damages. Yesterday morning, Judge Shen opened a hearing and brought Zhang Qingxiang, Zhang Quansheng, and Zhang (surname Zhang) to the case to announce the judgment. Zhang Qingxiang and Zhang Quansheng were both sentenced to death for jointly premeditating murder and deprived of their civil rights indefinitely. Zhang (surname Zhang) was sentenced to two years of imprisonment for joint murder. The defendants were jointly and severally liable to compensate Zhang Bao for 5,352 yuan for living expenses and 400 yuan for funeral expenses, and to compensate Zhang Guoxiang for 280 yuan for medical expenses and 500 yuan for consolation money. However, Zhang (surname Zhang) was temporarily released on bail during the appeal period, while Zhang Qingxiang and Zhang Quansheng were strictly guarded and shackled in the detention center.

Anti-Opium Society

Releases the Evils of Opium Monopoly

The rumor of opium monopoly has been rampant recently. The Chinese National Anti-Opium Society is very concerned and has continued to resist. The society yesterday released the disastrous situation of opium monopoly in various colonial areas in Southeast Asia to arouse the attention of the people of the country. The general idea is that today, countries that implement opium monopoly are only in colonies, including Japan in Taiwan and the Kwantung Leased Territory, Britain in Hong Kong, the Straits Settlements, the Malay Peninsula, etc., the Netherlands in the East Indies, Portugal in Macau, and France in Annam. Except for Annam, the society has sent personnel to investigate all the above places. The actual situation can be summarized in a few words. Japan [Opium monopoly is only collecting taxes without prohibition.] The government protects illegal murderous businesses with laws, encourages people to commit suicide and murder with the government's power, and collects profits from it. The victims are overseas Chinese and indigenous people. Now let's give a few examples to prove the evils of opium monopoly: (1) My country is known as the "country of opium." According to the society's estimate, the people who smoke opium account for 5% of the total population, at most no more than 10%. In the Straits Settlements of British Malaya, the number of overseas Chinese reaches 20% to 30%. This proves that opium monopoly will increase the number of opium smokers. (2) The opium prohibition in Taiwan is praised by those who advocate monopoly in my country and try to get the government to follow suit according to law. However, the results of opium prohibition over the past 30 years are ridiculous. In 1897, there were 50,597 opium smokers. By 1930, these 50,000 opium smokers should have died out due to age. Unexpectedly, in the same year, a new registration was made, and there were still more than 26,000 public smokers and more than 25,000 private smokers, totaling more than 2,000 additional people. And those not included in the statistics are not included. This shows that opium monopoly cannot reduce the number of opium smokers. (3) The total number of overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia is only more than 5 million. In 1928, the governments of British, French, and Dutch colonies imported 7,487 boxes of Indian and Persian opium for monopoly use, totaling 19,068,320 taels. If it is believed that opium monopoly is a scientific opium prohibition method, then the above places, which have been implementing monopoly for 20 to 30 years, still need more than 20 million taels of opium to supply the more than 5 million overseas Chinese people. In addition to expanding opium sales, what are the results of opium prohibition? (4) According to reliable statistics from the Singapore government, only 17% of the overseas Chinese who smoke opium brought their addiction from their home country, and 83% became addicted after arriving in the local area. This proves that the environment created by opium monopoly not only cannot make them quit opium, but actually drives people to become addicted. (5) In 1928, the Straits Settlements of British Malaya seized 3.2 million taels of opium smuggled by illegal immigrants. This shows that government monopoly cannot eliminate smuggling. (6) According to the report of the Malayan Opium Investigation Committee in 1924, almost all Chinese coolies smoke opium. These opium smokers live a life worse than cattle and horses, and spend more than 60% of their income on opium. These overseas Chinese are mostly trapped by opium addiction and cannot return to their home country for the rest of their lives in a foreign land. If we cite the above facts, we can see that the success of the opium monopoly policy lies in the money exchanged for the blood and sweat of poor, ignorant people. (7) The above examples are mostly from colonies where the government monopolies opium. The evils are so great. Even in my country, the former Opium Prohibition and Investigation Office and the official-merchant joint-stock monopoly organized by some people today will be even more unbearable. The above simple examples can show the harm of opium monopoly. Instead of calling it a scientific opium prohibition method, it is better to call it a scientific poisoning method. If we look at it from a scientific perspective, its results and effects are completely contrary to opium prohibition. Opium monopoly is a method of imperialist oppression of weak nations. If we recognize this as a scientific value, then we will be deceiving ourselves. If we recognize this as a good law and beautiful intention, it is actually neither good nor beautiful. Today, opium addiction is rampant in our country, there is no need to hide it. If the government has no determination to prohibit opium, how can we expect results? If the government is sincere, it should speak and act, and start with what it can do. For example, in Jiangbei, which is close to the capital, and Henan, where the acting capital is located, opium seedlings are everywhere. The special tax office of the two lakes, which violates the law, continues to exist. All kinds of things are enough to show that the authorities have no intention of prohibiting opium. It is not that opium cannot be prohibited. The current opium prohibition laws in our country are already very complete. The 44 motions passed by the first national opium prohibition conference are also very thorough. What is needed is only the determination and courage of the government authorities to earnestly implement them. Today, some people say that there is no way to prohibit opium, which is a big mistake. Today, it is not that there is no way, but that there are no people who abide by and enforce the law. The society's opposition to monopoly and supervision of opium prohibition is an unwavering and unchangeable principle. At this time of lax opium prohibition, we should work harder to follow the people of the country and fight to the end against the evil system of monopoly.

Songjiang District

Decision to Increase Salt Tax Rate

Shanghai Concession Increases by One Yuan Four Jiao Five Per Shi

Five Grades of High and Low Increase by One Jiao for Two Yuan Seven

Song District Can Earn Additional 500,000 After Tax Increase

Guowen News Agency reports that Finance Minister Song Ziwen has reorganized the salt tax and proposed a temporary tax rate for the reorganization of salt tax in the producing area. It has been passed by the Central Political Conference, and the Ministry of Finance has begun to implement it. The first phase of the reorganization area is the five districts of Liangzhe Songjiang, Huainan, Huaibei, and Changlu. Shanghai belongs to the Songjiang district, so yesterday the reporter specially visited the Songjiang Salt Transport Deputy Envoy's Office to inquire, and the details obtained are as follows:

Song District Salt Administration: The Songjiang Transport Envoy governs the five prefectures of Su, Chang, Zhen, Tai, and Song. The Song prefecture includes Chuannan, Bao, and the concession. In the past, the salt tax rate varied from high to low. After the audit office rectified it, in terms of the Song district, the tax per shi was 2.7 yuan in 18 counties and 3.2 yuan in 6 counties. However, the salt tax rate in Songjiang remained the same, with five grades of 3.2, 2.7, 1.5, and 1.6 yuan. The entire district produces and sells 3 million shi annually, and the concession produces 200,000 shi. The total annual income is about 4-5 million yuan.

Concession Tax Increase: The office has received instructions to increase the salt tax in the Shanghai concession. The original tax per shi was 1.5 yuan, and now the tax will be increased by 1.45 yuan, including all miscellaneous taxes, totaling 4.5 yuan per shi of salt produced. The Su and Chang prefectures in the Song district will not be increased, and the salt tax in Zhen and Tai will not be increased for those at 3.2 yuan, and will be increased by 1 jiao for those at 2.7 yuan. Chuannan Jiandi in the Song prefecture and Baoshan Jie will also be increased by 1 jiao for 19 liang diagrams. The rest will be increased by more than 1 yuan, but the number is not large.

Increased Amount: After the Song district implements the tax increase this time, the concession area, calculated at half a yuan per shi, can increase revenue by 300,000 yuan. The remaining prefectures, with some increasing and some not, can increase by about 200,000 yuan. These 50 million yuan are part of the 6 million yuan directly increased by the Ministry of Finance after this reorganization.

Implementation of Collection: The office has been ordered to actively proceed. Yesterday, it issued a notice to the collection agencies under its jurisdiction and discussed the collection methods with the Salt Affairs Audit Branch. The implementation date is said to be undetermined, but it is likely that the collection will be based on the increased amount starting next month.

Ministry and Provincial Governments Compete to Collect Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax

City Chamber of Commerce Advocates Tax Payment Temporarily Deposited in Bank

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce received a letter from the Local Yellow Wine Industry Association inquiring about the tobacco and alcohol license tax, which is collected by the Ministry and provincial governments separately. Which is the formal agency? Please investigate and instruct so that we can follow, etc. The association immediately replied, "The association has submitted this matter to the Ministry of Finance, inquiring about how to deal with the fact that the Jiangsu Province has established a bureau to collect taxes without the approval of the Ministry. At the same time, we have also notified the third district tobacco and alcohol license tax sub-bureau of Jiangsu Province that this case is currently being submitted to the Ministry for instructions. Before the Ministry's approval, it is not convenient to advise tobacco and alcohol merchants to change to the provincial bureau for tax collection. Your industry's tax payment continues to be paid to the Ministry in accordance with the procedures and does not violate the law. If you are worried about the entanglement between the bureau and the province, then follow the method of the Liang Shaoyu industry and deposit the tax payment in the Bank of China and send a letter to the two sub-bureaus of the Ministry and the province. This matter is to wait for the Ministry's instructions to determine which direction it belongs to before complying. The above two methods can be considered and implemented by your association," etc.
