Deadline for Changing Land Certificates

Order to Inform All Households in Map 1 Land Ziwei in Huning District

The Municipal Land Bureau announced yesterday, "For the purpose of announcement, after investigating the old 25th Bao Fourth Map in the Huning District, it has now been reorganized into Map 1 Land Ziwei in the Huning District. Since the land certificates of each household in the Wei began to be exchanged on September 16th of the 18th year of the Republic (1929), most of the property owners have complied with the payment of single strings to collect the land certificates. However, there are still some who have delayed collecting the drawings. According to the 14th article of the bureau's rules for issuing land practice certificates, it should have been reported to the Municipal Government for punishment. Considering that the property owners are scattered in all directions, the previous announcement may not have been fully informed. The Municipal Government has previously approved an extension of one year, and it has been more than a year. According to the case, the land of all households that have not exchanged certificates will be publicly auctioned or taken over by the city. However, the city suffered from war before, and transportation was inconvenient, resulting in exceeding the extended deadline. Now, in particular, a concession is given. Starting from the date of this announcement, the deadline is within three months to collect the property ownership certificate and go to the bureau to exchange the certificate. If there is any further delay, a punishment will be given," etc.

Municipal Council Promises

Free Clean Water to Help Poor People Prevent Epidemics

Yesterday (Wednesday), the Municipal Council Board of Directors approved the recommendation of the Health Committee. In order to assist in preventing cholera, the public concession water company was specially authorized to make concessions on the water price contract, so that some clean water could be provided free of charge to poor residents. The water company also sent a letter to the Municipal Council, promising to supply residents without water pipes on the road's fire hydrants as usual, and there would be no time limit. At the same time, the Health Department also investigated and gave water at several locations, all of which were areas where cholera was more severe. It was found that this matter had been suggested by the publicity team of the Shanghai Epidemic Prevention Conference, and the director of the fire brigade had drafted several methods. However, according to the director of the Health Department, free supply of clean water cannot completely prevent the spread of water, because there are still many wells everywhere, although disinfection has been carried out, but it is impossible to prevent washing vegetables and rice with river water and pond water. Also, there is no formal ratio between cholera statistics and unclean beverages, and residents' drinking water, those who do not get from tap water and artesian wells, are also less than 10%. Therefore, the director of the Health Department suggested that the free water supply can be approved in principle, but its implementation method and supply amount need to be carefully drafted. This idea was approved by the Health Committee, but if the expenditure is increased as a result, it must be submitted to the committee and the Board of Directors again. This recommendation was approved by the Board of Directors. The publicity team of the Epidemic Prevention Conference also suggested purchasing a cheap film projector to promote epidemic prevention, but because there is no concrete plan, the Health Committee decided to postpone it.

Municipal Council

Procedures for Selling Public Land

Regarding the Municipal Council's sale of the remaining land at the corner of Fuzhou Road and Jiangxi Road, some newspapers have criticized its procedures. The Public Works Committee discussed this section on the 8th of this month and believed that the criticism was unreasonable. However, it is necessary to stipulate these procedures in principle. Therefore, a committee member suggested that in the future, the sale of remaining land should be advertised, and bids should be received for two months, so that buyers can discuss with their headquarters. Also, if valuable land is sold, in addition to publishing an announcement in the Gazette, advertisements should be published separately in the newspaper to ensure that everyone knows. This proposal has been approved by the Board of Directors.

Tangqiao, Pudong

The Bao Wei Tuan Kills Jiang Guohua

At about 8 pm the night before, the local Bao Wei Tuan member killed a person resembling an imposter cop in Tangqiao Zhen. Here is the record of the investigation:

Bing Gun Stop: At 8:45 pm the night before, there were four men wearing mismatched clothes walking around Chenjiazhai, south of Wangjiazhai in Tangqiao Zhen, Pudong. Yang, the platoon leader of the 2nd platoon of the Tangshu District Bao Wei Tuan, saw that these people looked suspicious and immediately led a few members to stop these four men. He questioned them about the password and searched them one by one. The first three people had no prohibited items. Unexpectedly, one of the people in the back suddenly put both hands in his pocket and pulled out a box gun. Yang saw that the situation was not good and immediately opened the pistol and shot the person. Two shots hit the right shoulder, and the bullet penetrated backward. One bullet hit the left waist and did not penetrate. He fell to the ground and died on the spot. The other three took the opportunity to escape.

Willing Police Symbol: The deceased was wearing an outer robe of Chao blue cloth trousers, an inner white short shirt, yellow cloth shorts, yellow cloth leggings, black socks, and Zhigong cloth shoes. Yang searched the deceased's body on the spot and found a row of bullets and a symbol of a volunteer police officer named Jiang Guohua in a certain district. The 3rd sub-office of the Public Security Bureau 3rd District, took them back to the office for verification, and Yang took back a box gun to the regiment headquarters. The situation was reported to the superiors for verification.

Wife's Sad Complaint: Yesterday, Dong, the director of the 3rd sub-office of the 3rd District, ordered the local Bao Zhu Gongsheng to petition the Local Court. At 5 pm, Prosecutor Yang was commissioned, along with his staff, to come to the scene to inspect. The examiner found that the deceased had been shot and killed. The body was handed over to the family for coffin collection. Then, according to the wife of the deceased, Chang, her husband's name was Jiang Guohua, from Shandong. She also stated the situation of being shot and killed and requested justice. The official ordered to go to the court for questioning at 9 am today.

Kong Guangfu Implicated in Wu Kaixian Case

Municipal Party Department Sends Letter to Court Clarifying

In the case of Zhou Zhongyi and others involving robbery and murder, which is being handled by the First Special District Local Court of this city, one of the defendants, Kong Guangfu, allegedly made statements implicating Wu Kaixian, a member of the Municipal Party Department. The court has sent a letter to the Municipal Party Department to inquire about this. It is heard that the Municipal Party Department has responded to the court with the following letter: "Regarding your letter No. 56, in which you stated that this court is handling the case of Zhou Zhongyi and others involving robbery and murder, and that the defendant Kong Guangfu testified that after Shi Jinkun was shot and killed on August 21st of the 16th year of the Republic of China, someone was entrusted to submit a request to the Shanghai Municipal Party Department to forward it to the Central Party Department for approval and issue a pension. The petition's signatory and whether Kong Guangfu entrusted someone to submit it, and whether Wu Kaixian, the current Standing Committee member of your Municipal Party Department, held a position in your Municipal Party Department in the 16th, 17th, and 18th years of the Republic of China all need to be investigated. We hereby request your Municipal Party Department to investigate and verify the name of the signatory of Shi Jinkun's petition and Wu Kaixian's positions year by year in the 16th, 17th, and 18th years, and respond as soon as possible, etc. In response to the above, regarding the case of Kong Guangfu's suspected murder, it was previously reported that Kong made accusations in the police station implicating Wu Kaixian, a member of this committee, as ordering the murder. We initially intended to send a letter to correct this, but the news also reported that Kong clarified in your court that his previous statements in the police station regarding Wu Kaixian, a member of the Municipal Party Department, were purely false accusations, and that Wu Kaixian had no involvement or suspicion of ordering the murder, so we disregarded it. During the period of party purification in the 16th year of the Republic of China, the former Labor and Peasant Department of this party had an employee named Kong Guangfu (not Kong Guangfu), but he left after only a few months. When Shi Jinkun was shot and killed, Kong Guangfu was no longer working in this party department. As for the claim that someone was entrusted to submit a request to the Shanghai Municipal Party Department to forward it to the Central Party Department for approval and issue a pension, this department was destroyed by rioters last year, and the files are lost, so there is no record to verify. The current Standing Committee member Wu Kaixian is not Hu Kaixian. Wu Kaixian served as the secretary of the Organization Department of this party department from April of the 16th year of the Republic of China to April of the 17th year. In May of the 17th year, he served as the head of the Organization Department. He assumed his current position in March of the 20th year. When Wu Kaixian was the secretary of the Organization Department, the head of the Organization Department was Leng Xin, the head of the Labor and Peasant Department was Zhou Zhiliao, and the Standing Committee members were Chen [blank], Pan Yizhi, and Huang Huiping. At that time, each department handled its own affairs independently, and the secretary's position was responsible for internal documents and other matters, with no interference in external affairs. Wu Kaixian had no authority to handle affairs of other departments or direct the work of staff in other departments, so there is no basis to suspect him of ordering the murder. We hereby reply accordingly, hoping for your consideration. Furthermore, Zhang Guomin and others have never held positions in this party. The report that they are also staff members of this party department is clearly inaccurate. We hereby declare this in conjunction. Respectfully addressed to the First Special District Local Court of Jiangsu Shanghai."

Port Quarantine Office Cholera Weekly Report

Ships from Tianjin, Xiamen, Shantou, and Other Ports to be Quarantined from Today

Wu Liande of the Port Quarantine Office issued the seventh cholera weekly report yesterday (the 13th). The translation is as follows: '(1) In the past week, up to July 9th, the weather has been getting hotter every day. The highest indoor temperature reached 93.2 degrees Fahrenheit, and the highest temperature was 99 degrees (still one degree away from the highest [saturation] temperature). This week (July 2nd to 9th), a total of 317 cholera cases were discovered, with 21 deaths. The breakdown is listed below:

(District) (Cases) (Deaths)

Shanghai City 120 5

Public Concession 150 (including 13 (including

two foreigners) two foreigners)

French Concession 47 (including one 3 (including one

foreigner) foreigner)

Previous 1020 61

Total 1337 82 (including 7 foreigners)

(2) From the above, it can be seen that the cholera mortality rate in Shanghai this time is still low, only 6.1%. Among the 130 cases, 9 cases had been vaccinated before the onset of the disease, so all 9 cases were cured and recovered. (3) According to reports from medical officers serving in the war zones, such as Baoshan, Dachang, Lishan, and Jiading, there are approximately 2,000 wells in Baoshan County, but no cholera outbreaks have occurred yet. The residents of the other three counties rely entirely on river water for drinking water, so 40 cholera cases have been discovered, with 30 deaths. (4) Among the eight epidemic hospitals in Shanghai, the Xizang Road epidemic hospital has the most patients. According to Dr. Deng's report from the hospital, there have been 6 miscarriages (4 to 8 months pregnant) discovered among the female patients in the hospital. (5) The reassuring news is that the Shanghai Waterworks Company (Public Concession) has now installed 26 free water taps in poor areas to provide free water. The Public Concession Board of Works has also donated 5 water trucks and all spare parts to the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau for transporting water to poor areas. The Board of Works' enthusiasm is truly commendable. It is hoped that the effectiveness of this measure will be as significant as the implementation of vaccination. (6) Recently, the epidemic has spread widely in the cities of Dalian, Yingkou, and Henan, Shanxi in the northeast, as far as Xuyuan. Therefore, the traffic on the Longhai Railway (western Henan) has been temporarily cut off. According to the above, the cholera mortality rate in these ports is very high, reaching 50% to 80%. (7) Because cholera has already spread in Hong Kong, Guangzhou, Shantou, Xiamen, Tanggu, and Tianjin, this office has announced that these ports are epidemic ports from July 14th. All ships arriving in Shanghai from these ports must raise the quarantine flag (yellow flag) upon arrival and wait for inspection. All passengers, crew members, and sailors must undergo quarantine. Before receiving a traffic permit issued by the quarantine medical officer, they must not leave the ship and go ashore to emphasize the importance of epidemic prevention."

Shipping News

Collision Case Opens - The British ship collided with and sank the Texaco oil tanker "Keta Huai" and damaged the wharf, resulting in huge losses. This matter has been recorded in this newspaper. The harbor master of the Jianghai Customs summoned the captains and pilots of each ship yesterday at the customs to investigate the responsibility. First, he asked the captain of the "Keta Huai" to report the process of the collision, and then asked the Jianghai pilot Lin Guoying of the British ship "Pudeng." Lin said that the "Pudeng" ship collided with the "Keta Huai" because the "Chengdu" ship at the stern pushed it, leaving no room for maneuver, and causing the disaster. The case still requires investigation of the facts and will be continued to be heard. The port authority has not announced the results of the first trial.

Tax on Small Packages - Ships in the Yangtze River often have crew members and waiters who privately carry goods without paying freight. This is called "small packages." The ship authorities have repeatedly rectified this, but they often superficially comply. There are even more "small packages" on the Ningbo Yangtze River ships. The Jianghan Customs has imposed a small package tax because the ships' small packages do not pay freight or customs duties, resulting in huge annual losses. This has been notified to the ships for investigation. The shipping company has already held a meeting to discuss and implement strict regulations to crack down on this.

Construction Worker Tragically Drowns

Zhang Hongren, 27 years old, from Qingjiang, worked as a laborer at the British American Tobacco Company. Yesterday at 5 PM, he went swimming in the Huangpu River at the Qiwu Pulu Pier in Yangshupu. Unexpectedly, he was not skilled in swimming and suddenly drowned. He was rescued by the water police, taken to the hospital for treatment, but died.

Robbery on Baker Road Leads to Sentencing

The robbers Han Awu, Dai Mingzhi, and others, because they colluded in gangs with weapons between May and June of this year, robbed Xue Yinji inside the Baker Road unmarked house, Yin Baoming inside the 155 Parker Road house, and the householder Ren Zhuolin at 824 Wuchang Road, and stole gold and silver jewelry worth more than 1,000 yuan, escaped with the loot, and were at large. Until recently, the Red Mouth police detectives successively arrested Han and others, along with the woman Liu You and a pistol, 13 bullets, and escorted them to the First Special District Local Court. After repeated hearings, the trials concluded. Yesterday morning, when the sentence was due, the police escorted the defendants to the case, and Judge Shen ascended the seat and announced the sentence. Dai Mingzhi and Li Jinbao were each sentenced to 8 years of imprisonment, Han Awu and Chen Ershan were each sentenced to 7 years of imprisonment, and Liu You was sentenced to 6 months of imprisonment. The number of days in custody before the judgment was determined to be deducted from the sentence, with two days counted as one day. The guns and bullets were confiscated.

Incoming Mail

Declaration of the Chinese Civil Rights Promotion Association

Ma Xiangbo

Three Discussions on Land: Our country is known as an ancient country, and the world knows it. Next to all big mountains and big waters, there must be a certain number of li and zhang that are owned by the country. Otherwise, forests, waterways, and national defense cannot be managed.

State Association Successful, the central government has the right to make land deeds, cities and towns, or three mu, two mu, one mu is one deed, farmland, or fifty mu, thirty mu, fifteen mu is one deed, each county depending on trade, and fertile and special.

Deed tax, four yuan per sheet, retained for each county to set up agricultural, industrial, and commercial official banks, and poor households can borrow coupons to purchase it. In this way, even the poorest counties can have three agricultural, industrial, and commercial banks, and the people are not strong enough, how can the country be rich and strong? This is an ancient training. In addition to the four yuan, add a paper registration fee of fifty cents, and the central government and each county divide it into two or three equal parts.

Counties, prefectures, and states each have treasuries and banks, county banks are directly connected to the people, so their power is greatest, county banks can also directly invest in domestic, large factories, large mines, large buildings, for the savings of county treasuries, the so-called large buildings, such as opening rivers, opening roads, opening forests, etc., are all. In addition to the first year of collecting four and a half yuan, the number of deed taxes will be more than tens of thousands, even public properties such as government offices must have a deed, no exceptions. All customs duties on passengers and goods, using one-tenth of each county's money and grain, are all attributed to the central government, because foreign affairs and foreign invaders are all handled by the central government.

In addition to one-tenth of each county's money and grain being attributed to the central government, two-tenths being attributed to the prefecture, and one-tenth being attributed to the state, the remaining six-tenths are all attributed to local autonomy, and cultural and military preparations.

All states, prefectures, and counties that support the above-mentioned legal methods are regarded as state associations, otherwise, the imperial crusade doctrine must not be used to thoroughly provoke private grievances and private affairs, and hurt the feelings of fellow countrymen, it must be firmly remembered, the clear teachings of those who overcome others with force are not convinced, but they must not be affiliated with foreign countries other than China, or other [blank] to compete with my China for this land (End).

Shenbao Local Supplement

Speech

Obligatory Work During Summer Vacation

— Tian

It is now early July, and most schools have already started their summer vacation. Here are some suggestions for students to consider during the summer vacation, for the academic community to study.

(1) Distributing Printed Materials. Although there are many new books and newspapers being published, they are limited to certain areas and cannot reach everyone. Someone once said, "The current cultural movement is an aristocratic cultural movement," which is a poignant statement. However, I believe that even the aristocratic aspect cannot truly become widespread. I don't think there's much optimism for this narrow and weak cultural movement. Seeing this, we must think of ways to remedy it. This summer vacation provides us with a good opportunity to vigorously promote cultural endeavors. Suppose we distribute easily understandable printed materials, publishing articles that are closely related to the readers. On the one hand, we can collect valuable and interesting articles from classmates and show them to others. This will not only spark their interest but also guide them to improve their writing. However, there are many things to consider when distributing such printed materials. Here are a few points:

Printing: It is best to use letterpress printing if possible; otherwise, mimeographing is also acceptable. The most important thing is that it should be clear and legible.

Binding: If it is letterpress printing, the format of the Saturday newspaper can be followed. If it is mimeographed, it is best to staple it into a small booklet so that people who read it don't easily lose it.

Pricing: It is best if it can be distributed completely free of charge, without charging a single cent. If there are financial difficulties, the price should be set at the lowest possible level, because we must adopt a spirit of sacrifice when running this type of newspaper.

Material: Of course, the focus should be on the common people, to give them a sense of class consciousness. In areas with many merchants, more articles about merchant awareness and apprentice liberation can be included. In areas with many farmers and workers, more articles related to farmers and workers should be included. In short, adapt to local conditions and strive to be practical.

Style: Use entirely vernacular Chinese so that everyone can understand.

Signature: Do not sign anything to avoid others saying that we are showing off. The responsibility for publishing articles should be borne jointly by the organizers.

(2) Summer Obligatory Schools. Everyone knows that to improve society, we must first popularize education. To popularize education, everyone knows that we must promote obligatory schools. But obligatory schools! This call has been made for many years, but how many have actually been opened? We can barely find a few in cities, and they have virtually no impact in rural areas! Everyone! We must not just engage in empty talk. Let's be down-to-earth and do our best to actually do it. Our hometowns should have at least one or two obligatory elementary schools. We can borrow equipment from local elementary schools, and we can also borrow the buildings of local elementary schools. The equipment and rental costs can all be saved. As long as we spend a few hours a day, we can give those ignorant compatriots the opportunity to learn to read and study.

(3) Practice Labor. We talk about the sacredness of labor every day and read books about the sacredness of labor. But let's ask ourselves, have we actually practiced labor ourselves at all? It's truly shameful! I advocate washing clothes, cleaning roads, etc. We must all put these things into practice, not just to save a few coins or use fewer servants. It can also exercise our muscles and bones, put our labor ideology into practice, and smash the signboard of the young master and government official. Furthermore, if we can gather a few classmates and live together during this period, preparing all the food ourselves, it will not only cultivate an independent character, but also create a lot of interest!

Literature and Art

Fleeing from Disaster

— Wu Yucang

On March 2nd of this year, threatened by Japanese aircraft bombing, I moved with the old and young, wandering and fleeing, and arrived at Beishendian Bridge in Shaxi Town on the 18th. I resided in the home of a farmer surnamed Su. As time passed, I recorded my experiences and showed them to friends to tell of my suffering. I record my journey covered in dust, my lodgings have changed several times. The scenery is so bleak, the season is still Qingming. The chaotic world is also very poor, and the old farmers still till the land with hardship. I am ashamed to spread words idly, with no plan to benefit the people's livelihood. I arrived in a hurry to escape the invaders, meeting only old friends. They earnestly offer food and drink, and laughter and words comfort my hardships. It is hard to bear the sight of scars everywhere, and hard to hold back tears. We all share responsibility for the rise and fall, and I am ashamed to be spared. Where is the Peach Blossom Spring? Fortunately, I found a secluded place to live. The market is far away, and there are few guests and friends. The customs are simple, and etiquette is sparse. I foolishly talk about staying as an old farmer in the countryside, enjoying new vegetables with healthy meals. I cannot ask about the road ahead, entrusting my fleeting life to fate. Although I have lost my place in this displacement, it is not enough to lament the difficulties. My impoverished escape has unexpectedly strengthened me, and I feel at peace living in the wilderness. I sometimes read books by the fence and occasionally hold a fishing rod by the stream. I am deeply ashamed of stealing leisure, lacking the talent to reverse the tide.

Also sent to my second younger brother, Yulin

Counting the days, we have been separated for three months, and I send my longing in a letter from thousands of miles away.

Laughter and words before the lamp often linger in my dreams, and the scenes of the calamity are half in poetry.

Take care of yourself in the lonely inn, and I will support my aging mother at home.

The cuckoo in Jiangguan cries out repeatedly, asking when the returning boat will arrive.

It is precisely in middle age that one has many feelings, and again I see the situation in chaos like hemp.

Brothers bickering among themselves plot against each other, and jackals and wolves lurk, sucking blood flowers.

A surge of solitary indignation should strike the oars, and a man can make his home anywhere in the world.

Do you know if we often think of each other at the ends of the earth? Tonight, I finish composing the poem, and the moon is already setting.

Science

Portland Cement

— Ming

Cement mixed with gravel and sand becomes concrete, which is widely used in construction. There are many types of cement, the most important of which is Portland cement. Now, I will describe its raw materials, composition, manufacturing method, and setting.

(1) Raw Materials. The most common raw materials are limestone or marl, and clay or shale.

(2) Composition. The percentage of its main components is as follows:

Lime (CaO) 60-64.5 Average 62.0

Silica (SiO2) 20-24.0 Average 22.0

Alumina (Al2O3) 5-9.0 Average 7.5

Magnesia (MgO) 1-4.0 Average 2.5

Iron Oxide (Fe2O3) 2-4.0 Average 2.5

Sulfur Trioxide (SO3) 1-1.75 Average 1.5

Among them, the ratio of lime to silica, alumina, and magnesia is approximately 1.9 to 2.1. The ratio of silica to alumina is approximately 2.5 to 4. These two ratios are very important when manufacturing cement. If there is too much lime, the cement will expand and break during setting. If there is too little lime, the cement will set too slowly. If there is a lot of silica, it will set very slowly. If there is a lot of alumina, it will set very quickly.

(3) Manufacturing. Mix the above raw materials according to their composition, grind them into a fine powder, and load them into a furnace (the temperature in the furnace is approximately 1450 to 1600 degrees Celsius). Heat them until they are close to the melting point. The resulting gray lumps are called clinker. Take them out and cool them, then crush them into powder. However, clinker sets very quickly, so gypsum is usually added, about 2% or 3% of the weight of the clinker, and ground finely at the same time as the clinker. Gypsum has the effect of inhibiting the setting of cement and is called a negative catalyst.

(4) Setting. Cement can turn into a hard, stone-like substance after adding water. This is because the clinker contains components such as (CaO)2·SiO(CaO)3·SiO2(CaO)2·Al2O3 and (CaO)3·Al2O3. When they come into contact with water, they become hydrates. These hydrates are crystalline and can turn into hard blocks.

Family Matters

The Flavor of a Large Family

— Meng Yuan

The Shen mansion in P Town is considered one of the leading large families! The house employs many old maids and servant girls. Their lives ought to be comfortable and harmonious with everyone catering to their needs, which is a human's most happy living. However, the reality is the opposite, with many disputes often occurring in their home.

According to rumors from people inside the Shen mansion, the reason for the quarrels is all due to the Second Young Mistress. The Second Young Mistress was married by the Second Young Master last year. She is a graduate of the XX Women's Normal School and is presumably very knowledgeable! However, she doesn't understand anything about family matters. Every day, she just puts on makeup and orders servants around. The Old Madam (an eighteenth-century old woman) doesn't think this is right. She believes that a daughter-in-law is supposed to help with household affairs. What's the use if she can't do anything? Is she just here to eat and do nothing? (She doesn't know that new-style women in the twentieth century are all like this.) Therefore, she can't help but grumble behind her back!

The Second Young Mistress is truly full of airs, a modern woman. Besides putting on makeup, eating, she also plays cards and mahjong. She treats her husband as a bank and her family as a hotel. The more highly educated a woman is, the more she does this.

Therefore, the Old Madam often complains about her behind her back, scolding her for just eating, dressing, and playing every day, without understanding anything about the household affairs, not even knowing the proper greetings for elders. She has never paid her respects once, truly an uncultured woman.

The Second Young Mistress is such a proud person, how could she not get angry when she heard these words? Therefore, she often cursed, saying, "The Old Madam is an old antique, a confused old woman, a stupid thing from the twentieth century. It's enough that I have food to eat and clothes to wear every day. Why do I need someone to manage some household affairs?"

As a result, the rift between the mother-in-law and daughter-in-law deepened. Recently, the Second Young Mistress returned home, and the Old Madam happily said, "Now that she's gone, I can live in peace!"

Later, the Second Young Master sent a letter asking her (the Second Young Mistress) to go to S Port, but the Second Young Mistress didn't even go home to explain, she just went to S Port on her own!

After living in S Port for two months, the Second Young Master wanted to return to his hometown to see his family, but the Second Young Mistress refused to come with him. He couldn't do anything about it, so he had to let her go!

Ah! This is the so-called flavor of a large family with servants catering to one's needs!

A Corner of Society

The Lesson of Boarding the Train

— Yuezhong Xiaocan

"The train is coming soon!" A road guard in a yellow uniform shouted like this, he continued to say to a customer in a suit, "Hey! Sir! Please step forward, the train is coming, you will be hit!"

Woo... Woo... In the eardrums of every passenger, the train sounded far and near, the objects placed on the ground, all in orderly fashion, were picked up to prepare for the train to stop at the station, immediately go up, and find a comfortable seat.

Squeak... Squeak... The train pulled into the station, and the porter on the third carriage stuck his head out of the window and shouted, "Back!" "Back is empty!" But the passengers didn't care whether it was the front or the back, they just scrambled to get on.

The classmates traveling together were also scattered at that moment, only the leader, Mr. Xie, and I were still together.

"Did you hear that! The porter said the back is empty! Let's go to the back, shall we!" Mr. Xie asked me like this.

"Okay, okay, let's go to the back, it's good that the back is empty!" I replied casually.

Arrived at carriage I, then carriage II, the porter in the window similarly stuck his head out and shouted, "Back!" "Back is empty!" We followed his instructions and walked back two more carriages, all of which were second class, but as we walked, the porter stuck his head out and similarly shouted, "Back!" "Back is empty!" We walked straight to the last carriage, and he was still shouting, "Back!"

"Back is empty!" At this time, we were really sweating profusely from walking and couldn't walk anymore.

With a "woo" sound, the train started moving, and we had to reluctantly jump into the last carriage. Once we got on the train, the reality told us that the porter was a truthful guide.

"We've been tricked! We've been tricked! It would have been better if we had boarded the front carriages earlier. The porter said 'the back is empty,' where is the emptiness? Terrible, terrible," Mr. Xie said regretfully like this.

"Alas! Really, we've been tricked. We walked so much, sweated so much, and couldn't find a seat, so we had to insert candles. But we've suffered this time, next time we'll learn to be smarter."

The court has sealed and appraised the following property owned by the debtor. The auction is scheduled for 12:00 PM on July 18th. The court will dispatch a clerk to direct the bailiff to conduct the auction. Anyone who wishes to buy this property should immediately report to the bailiff's office of this court to be led to the location for viewing and then follow the schedule to bid. If there are two or more bidders, the bidder with the highest price will be the buyer. The full price must be paid on the spot, and the auctioned property will be given for receipt. This notice is hereby given. (Details included) (1) Object of the auction: Movable property (list attached separately). (2) Location of the property: 379 and 375 Tongfu Road. (3) Minimum price: A total of 73 foreign dollars. (4) Location for viewing the records: Bailiff's office of this court. (5) Executing Clerk: Wang Zhen, Bailiff: Lu Zhaoxiong. (Above dated July 13th)

▲Civil Judgments: Ma Xianxun versus Ding Chen Shi and others regarding land lease (Main Text): The portion of land located at No. 280, 24th Regiment, 24th Bao, Shanghai, should be used by the plaintiff to build a house, and the defendants must not obstruct it. The litigation costs are to be borne equally by the defendants. ▲Gao Shouqing versus Wanchun Teahouse and others regarding rent arrears (Main Text): The defendant Wanchun Teahouse should pay the plaintiff rent of $378. The defendants Wanchun Shun Hao and Chen Shunqing should pay the plaintiff rent of $20. The defendant Yongyuanchang should repay the plaintiff rent of $160. The plaintiff is permitted to retain the assets of each of the aforementioned defendants. Litigation costs, excluding the one-sixth portion withdrawn, which is borne by the plaintiff, and the two-sixth portion settled separately, the remaining three-sixths are to be borne proportionally by the respective defendants. ▲Ruling on the case of Wang Heting versus Jin Bosheng regarding river port application (Main Text): The application is rejected. The application fee is to be borne by the applicant. ▲Wang Chen Shi versus Zhang Mingzhao and others regarding compensation for damages (Main Text): The defendants shall jointly and severally compensate the plaintiff for damages of $1,000. The remainder of the plaintiff’s claim is rejected. The first item of this judgment (Main Text) is approved for immediate execution. The litigation costs are to be borne jointly and severally by the defendants. ▲Shen He Gao versus Wang Xiaomao and others regarding gasoline (Main Text): The defendants Wang Xiaomao and Zhu Chengsheng should each repay one-third of the 150 gallons of gasoline to the plaintiff, or pay the plaintiff in cash at the market price. The remainder of the plaintiff’s claim is rejected. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendants Wang Xiaomao and Zhu Yongsheng by two-tenths each, and the plaintiff by sixteen-tenths. ▲Shen Juquan versus Lu Damao regarding debt arrears (Main Text): The defendant should repay the plaintiff 201 yuan and 7 jiao on behalf of Jiufeng Meat Shop. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant. ▲Cai Zhongji and others versus Wang Rong regarding redemption of house appeal (Main Text): The original judgment is overturned. The redemption price of the house located at Wubu Bridge is set at 380,000 wen. The appellant should redeem it from the appellee for a cash price of 1,090 wen plus 5 wen, equivalent to one silver dollar. The litigation costs for the first and second trials are to be borne by the appellant. ▲Wu Song’e versus Chen Shilin regarding land appeal (Main Text): The part of the original judgment regarding the demolition of the steps built by the defendant along the north side of the disputed land and restoration of the original state is overturned. The appellee's claim in the first instance regarding the aforementioned part is rejected. The litigation costs for the first and second trials are to be borne by both parties separately. ▲Song Hongsheng versus Song Guozhou and others regarding loan (Main Text): The defendant should repay the plaintiff $350. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant. ▲Chen Shunqing versus Chen Baosheng regarding loan (Main Text): The defendant should repay the plaintiff 500 silver dollars and 500 silver dollars in interest. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant. ▲Zhuang Shunlin versus Zhai Lizhang regarding rent arrears. The defendant should repay the plaintiff rent of $38. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant. ▲Sheng Tela Mu versus Han Ji and others regarding loan (Main Text): The defendant Han Ji should pay the plaintiff $880. If unable to repay, the defendant Chen Shousong should be responsible for repaying $400. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant. ▲Ou Changqi versus Ou Jifang regarding land and coffin relocation cross-lawsuit (Main Text): The plaintiff's lawsuit and the defendant's counterclaim are both rejected. The litigation costs for the main lawsuit and the counterclaim are to be borne by both parties separately.

▲Criminal Directives: The petition of Li Chunfa to withdraw the case has been noted. Withdrawal of the accusation is approved. This directive. ▲The petition of Wang Zhou Shi to investigate the case has been noted. The disappearance of her son is not related to a criminal matter. How can she request an investigation? If she claims that he was murdered, she must bring forward concrete evidence before it can be investigated. She should be notified immediately. This directive. ▲The petition of Zhou Zhiyu for provincial release has been noted. He should be placed under proper guarantee and await provincial review. This directive.

▲Criminal Judgments: Zhuang Shulong and others theft case (Main Text): Zhuang Shulong, Yu A’da, Wang Changlin, Gao Xiaoniu, Zhang Youcai, Zhao Xiaoshu, Xu De are convicted of group theft with three or more people and are sentenced to six months of imprisonment each. The number of days detained will be calculated as two days of detention equal to one day of imprisonment. ▲Ruling on the case of Lu Shijie’s appeal (Main Text): This further appeal is rejected. ▲Ruling on the case of Zhu A’mao’s murder appeal (Main Text): The ruling made on June 28 of this year is revoked. ▲Tang Er’s case of obstructing freedom (Main Text): Tang Er is not guilty. ▲Peng Xiaochun and others’ case of interfering with family (Main Text): Peng Xiaochun and Peng Lu Shi are jointly convicted of enticing a woman under the age of twenty away from her guardian with the intention of making a profit, and are each sentenced to one year of imprisonment. The number of days detained will be calculated as two days of detention equal to one day of imprisonment. ▲Song Zhenxian’s opium case (Main Text): Song Xian is convicted of possessing opium with the intention of selling it and is sentenced to one year and one month of imprisonment. The number of days detained will be calculated as two days of detention equal to one day of imprisonment. Four bags of red pills, totaling 24 taels, and one package of prepared opium, totaling 4.5 qian, are confiscated.

▲Civil Judgments: Ye Pengyuan versus Liu Zhenhai and others regarding goods payment (Main Text): Defendant Zhao Guocan should pay the plaintiff for goods $11.27. Defendant Liu Zhenhai should pay the plaintiff for goods $63.25. The litigation costs are to be borne by defendant Liu Zhenhai by three-sixths and Zhao Guocan by one-sixth. ▲Yang Muying versus Zhou Wang Shi and others regarding severing family ties (Main Text): The plaintiff’s claim is rejected. The litigation costs are to be borne by the plaintiff. ▲Yang Dai Shi versus Yang Shutang regarding cohabitation (Main Text): The defendant should cohabitate with the plaintiff. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant. ▲Wang A’bao versus Zheng Kaijun regarding contract and guarantee money (Main Text): The plaintiff’s claim is rejected. The litigation costs are to be borne by the plaintiff. ▲Xu Hongbing versus Zhang Quanjin regarding tomb relocation fee (Main Text): The defendant should pay the plaintiff a tomb relocation fee of $190, plus annual interest of five percent from June 11, 1932 until the date of execution. The remainder of the plaintiff’s claim is rejected. The litigation costs are to be borne by the plaintiff by one-fourth and the defendant by three-fourths.

▲Civil Directives: The petition of Yao Shangzhen to sever father-son relationship and request registration has been noted. According to regulations, a head of household may separate adult or married family members from the household, but the separation only entails separation of property and separate living. The title of father and son cannot be severed. The petition states that he fears being implicated. If the son commits illegal acts, the son should be directly responsible, and there is no need to worry. The request for registration does not need to be discussed. This directive. ▲The petition of Yang Zhao Shi to request a postponement has been noted. On the 6th of this month, Yang Zhongying came to court and requested that the case funds be paid off by the 10th of next month, which was approved, and the creditor agreed. Now, he is petitioning for a two-month extension, which is inappropriate. He should follow the previously requested deadline to pay the funds. Do not delay the case. This directive. ▲The petition of Mu Jixiang to request strict enforcement has been noted. In this case, the agent of the debtor was summoned for execution on the 5th of this month and requested to repay half in installments. This court deemed it inappropriate and ordered full payment within one month. This does not harm the creditor’s rights. If there is any delay after the deadline, strict enforcement will be carried out. He should be notified immediately. This directive. ▲The petition of Gu Yunxiang and others to request compensatory purchase has been noted. He should come to the court at 10:00 AM on the 18th of this month to await interrogation.
